Japan Worries About Raising the Manchurian Question at the Washington Conference 74

Ishii Dreams of Cooperation Between China, Japan, and the Puppet Regime

The Lansing-Ishii Agreement is Revisited

Reuters, Tokyo, 22nd - Ishii, the Japanese representative who went to Washington to participate in the economic discussions, said to Japanese reporters today, I am convinced that although the Ishii-Lansing Agreement was repealed at the Washington Conference, its main principle, that is, the United States' recognition of Japan's prominent position in the Far East, is still understood by most of American public opinion. I do not know whether the Manchurian question will be mentioned in this Washington discussion, but I can say without a doubt that the Manchurian question has become a thing of the past. The key point for the world today is the unified cooperation between Japan (Manchukuo) and China in order to seek a way out of the current economic and social difficulties in the Far East. For the sake of maintaining peace in the Far East and world peace in general, this kind of cooperation is really necessary. The sooner China understands this point, the more beneficial it will be to the three countries, but if China does not understand it sooner, the Republic of China will inevitably fall into an irreparable predicament. (Reuters, 22nd)

Anglo-American Giants Meet at the White House 75

MacDonald Arrives in America with a Spirit of Amity and Cooperation

Claims America's Abandonment of the Gold Standard Will Not Affect Negotiations

US Government Decides on Policy for China Meeting

Refuses to Cancel War Debts, Focuses on Tax Rates

Supports Raising Silver Prices and Military Disarmament

Havas, New York, 21st – British Prime Minister MacDonald, accompanied by his daughter and members of the British delegation, arrived in New York at 10:30 this morning aboard the (Berengaria). British Ambassador to the US, Sir Ronald Lindsay, embassy staff, representatives from the State Department, and journalists boarded the ship to welcome them. MacDonald told the press that he came with a spirit of amity and cooperation, just as he did when he visited President Hoover in 1929. He added that the United States' abandonment of the gold standard would not affect his future talks with President Roosevelt, or at least that was his understanding based on the limited information he had. MacDonald then boarded a steamboat with Lindsay and others to cross the Hudson River. He did not disembark in New York, but went directly to Washington D.C. via a special train from Jersey City. During the journey, Ambassador Lindsay explained to MacDonald the situation created by the United States' abandonment of the gold standard. Upon arriving in Washington, MacDonald will immediately go to the White House, where President Roosevelt will host a banquet to welcome him. The first political discussion between Roosevelt and MacDonald will take place after the banquet. President Roosevelt had a slight cold a few days ago, but has fully recovered. He will accompany MacDonald on a cruise up the Potomac River on Sunday, where the two can hold secret talks. This is just like when Hoover invited MacDonald to the Rapidan camp for secret talks during MacDonald's previous visit to the United States. The public hopes that the talks will be filled with an atmosphere of intimacy and that both sides can understand each other.

Reuters, Washington, 21st – British Prime Minister MacDonald and his entourage arrived in the US capital tonight. They studied the recent developments in the United States during the train journey. Secretary of State Hull greeted them at the station and then escorted the guests to the White House. President Roosevelt, breaking precedent, welcomed them at the front porch with his wife and daughter, Mrs. Dahl. The British Prime Minister's address, broadcast from the Berengaria, has created a very good impression on the American people.

Havas, Washington, 21st – According to well-informed sources, the US government has decided on the attitude to be taken on various issues to be discussed in the upcoming Washington talks: (1) (War debt issue) The US government, in accordance with the Democratic Party platform, has no choice but to firmly reject the cancellation of war debts. However, it will not reject the reduction or temporary suspension of war debt payments. In the government's view, the war debt issue is just one part of the global economic situation. (2) (Currency issue) The US government believes that stabilizing exchange rates is a fundamental condition for revitalizing world trade. Therefore, the United States is prepared to revise tax rates, but other countries should also revise them at the same time. (3) (Silver price issue) The US government is prepared to discuss with various countries methods to raise silver prices, and if all countries adopt bimetallism, the United States is also prepared to consider it. (4) (Disarmament issue) The US government believes that the huge military expenditures borne by various countries are an obstacle to all efforts to restore economic equilibrium. Therefore, it will assist in any initiative to reduce armaments.

Anglo-American Negotiations Begin 76

National, Washington, 21st – British Prime Minister MacDonald and US President Roosevelt quietly began their arduous task of stabilizing the gold dollar and the gold pound and jointly fighting to save the economy from decline tonight in the White House reception room. The financial frenzy that has arisen around the world since the United States abandoned the gold standard was also fully dispelled when MacDonald set foot in the White House, as it is believed that the two countries will not engage in a war of currency inflation. Upon arriving in Washington, MacDonald told reporters that he wanted to discuss the international restoration of the gold standard and war debts with President Roosevelt as part of a comprehensive economic problem, but that he did not particularly focus on the war debt aspect. He also said that it was regrettable that some outside observers had made harsh comments about the United States' abandonment of the gold standard. He wanted to earnestly request the fullest cooperation between Britain and the United States on the current great undertaking. A Paris dispatch also indicated that Herriot was willing to participate in this effort to avoid causing a currency inflation war and to avoid isolating France. Herriot also sent a radio message from the Ile de France, stating that he was willing to do his best to cooperate to facilitate President Roosevelt's arduous work.

US Proposals 77

As for the talks between Roosevelt and MacDonald, it is said that Roosevelt will first propose reducing tariffs, concluding several reciprocal trade agreements between countries, and universally agreeing to special rights for countries to expand trade. Regarding the reduction of tariffs by the United States, Roosevelt will propose that other countries reduce them in the same way as a reward. He will also propose joint action by countries to curb the activities of exchange speculators, who often do not hesitate to depreciate their own or other countries' currencies for personal gain. As for the war debt issue, according to reliable sources, the President will not offer any other suggestions except for the one approved by Congress to allow debtor countries to repay a portion of their debts in silver in the first year. He only wants to listen quietly to Britain's proposals and then immediately consult with congressional leaders. If Congress believes that the financial situation and domestic public opinion allow for modification of war debts, then he will support the modification. In addition, the President will propose that governments of all countries use methods that do not violate the constitution and can be implemented to help raise prices.

British Proposals 78

As for British Prime Minister MacDonald, in addition to proposing the international restoration of the gold standard, he is expected to agree to the general reduction of tariffs and the careful adjustment of tariffs by various countries. It is also heard that MacDonald will insist that if tariffs are generally reduced, the principle of equality must be followed. However, this issue of equality is almost as difficult as the currency issue, because what Britain considers equal, the United States Congress may consider unequal. For example, there are many goods on which Britain levies a tax of 30 percent, while the United States levies 60 percent. However, what MacDonald wants is the real reduction of excessively high tax rates, while taxes levied solely for revenue purposes seem to be secondary. As for war debts, Britain now believes that previous agreements were not based on international equality. Therefore, MacDonald will demand that any new agreement, regardless of who makes it, must be based on equality, and he will describe a final solution that can be implemented once and for all. In resolving the issue, the so-called (prosperity index) should not be used as the basis, nor should the ability to pay be asked, because MacDonald believes that these two items change from time to time in various countries and cannot be used as the basis for resolution. As for financial issues, because of their important relationship with international commerce, it is said that they will be discussed first.

Roosevelt Quickly Seeks Passage of Currency Inflation Bill Through Congress 79

To Gain Sufficient Tools for Negotiations with Britain and France

Republicans Attempt to Obstruct, But May Not Succeed

France Expresses Determination Not to Abandon the Gold Standard

Germany Believes Dollar Depreciation is Beneficial to It

Reuters, Washington, 21st – It is expected that the President's limited currency inflation bill will pass quickly, so that the President will have sufficient tools when negotiating with British Prime Minister and others. Senator Robinson stated today after meeting with the President that appropriate debate in Congress will not be prevented, but if anyone engages in disruption and obstruction, the number of votes Congress can obtain will be sufficient to prevent it. The final passage of the rural relief bill will indeed require a slight delay, but the amendments to this bill must be dealt with quickly, as the United States will engage in economic discussions with foreign governments. Sharpened disputes have now developed.

Reuters, Paris, 22nd – French Finance Minister Bonnet told guests today that France will not abandon the gold standard. France's position is very clear. France hopes that various countries will restore the gold standard as soon as possible. The French cabinet has decided that the government should request that a world economic conference be convened as soon as possible. Instructions have already been sent to Herriot, the French representative to the preparatory meeting in Washington, ordering him to submit this proposal as soon as he arrives in Washington.

Reuters, Paris, 21st – Reuters learned today from responsible sources that France will not abandon the gold standard at present. However, according to the opinion of a certain French economist, if world prices cannot return to French domestic prices, France will be forced to abandon the gold standard due to heavy domestic debt burdens and significant export losses. He predicts that the current rate of imports of US goods will be immediately readjusted.

Reuters, Berlin, 21st – A communique was issued here today, expressing the opinion that Germany should be allowed to repay its dollar loans in paper dollars, saying that Germany should not disregard the gold clauses in its loan agreements. Because the United States can legally reduce the gold value of its own obligations while still maintaining the gold value of its claims, which is unfair.

National, Berlin, 21st – Financial circles here have issued a semi-official announcement, giving a detailed analysis of the current state of the international monetary system after the dollar's decline. The conclusion is that the current drop in the price of the dollar is not due to international trade or the movement of assets. This move is actually a strategy with far-reaching intentions by the US authorities. The announcement also said that the events in the United States may have an adverse impact on Germany's export industry. Because after the dollar falls, export goods can be sold at lower prices or aggressive dumping policies can be implemented. The previous example is the British abandonment of the gold standard, which is very obvious. However, Germany can also make a small profit, such as reducing external debts due to the lower price of gold dollars. As for Germany's response to the actions of the United States, there is absolutely no intention to imitate it. The German government will be able to adhere to the principles announced by the president of the national bank a few days ago, that the German people who deposit their savings in banks can rest easy. Because the national bank is being cautious everywhere and is trying to maintain the interests of depositors without endangering their deposits.

Currency Inflation Draft Passed by Senate Banking Committee 80

Havas, Washington, 21st – The Senate Banking Committee approved Roosevelt's currency inflation draft. Today, the committee began reviewing the bill with Treasury Secretary Woodin and Budget Director Douglas, barring outsiders from attending.

Reuters, Washington, 21st – The Senate Banking Committee today passed an amendment to the rural relief bill, containing the President's monetary plan. This amendment has now been sent to the House of Representatives for review. Some members of the committee suggested deleting the clause reducing the gold content of coins, but the votes were tied at ten for and ten against, so the motion failed to pass. However, a clause was passed allowing the Federal Reserve to instruct the reserve banks to increase or decrease the reserve requirements for their deposits as needed to curb inflation. The President personally indicated that the amendment to the rural relief bill should be enacted as soon as possible and that debate must be brief to avoid obstruction by the Republicans.

Opposition Party Stands Up to Fight and Obstruct the Government's Inflation Plan 81

Reuters, Washington, 21st – The Republicans today in the Senate criticized the authorities' plan. Opposition leader Reed claimed that the government's plan would inflate the currency by 200 billion yuan. The Federal Reserve could issue 30 billion yuan of currency in the open market, could print 30 billion yuan of paper money, could reduce the gold content of coins and increase the existing currency by 60 billion yuan, and could use the remaining gold certificates of 80 billion yuan. The Democrats replied that President Roosevelt had said earlier that the currency inflation plan was only to give the President the power to act judiciously. This kind of power may not be used if it is not needed.

President Consults with Silver Senators on the Issue of Issuing Silver Coins 82

Havas, Washington, 22nd – President Roosevelt and Senators King of Utah and Wheeler of Montana consulted on the silver issue for a long time. The US government seems prepared to issue silver coins, as the movement in Congress to use silver as currency is gaining momentum. The so-called (silver senators) (that is, senators from silver-producing states such as Colorado, Nevada, New Mexico, Texas, Utah, and Wyoming) are all advocating the use of silver as currency and are advocating that the President issue 60 billion yuan of exchange notes based on full-power laws, that is, as silver exchange notes, which are fully guaranteed by silver. It is also said that the existing silver in the United States is only enough to guarantee 10 billion yuan of exchange notes, and that issuing 60 billion yuan of exchange notes would not only allow the silver mines that are currently closed to reopen, but the Treasury Department would also have to purchase silver from foreign countries. If so, countries such as Mexico and China that store silver can re-export silver. As silver prices rise, the price of their domestic currencies will also increase. It is found that Mexico and China are the important customers of the United States. They currently lack the ability to purchase American goods. If silver prices are raised, these countries can restore their prosperity. Therefore, raising silver prices has a major task in relieving the economic decline of the United States.

Reuters, Washington, 21st – The silver clause in the currency inflation bill drafted by Senators King and Wheeler stipulates that the President has the right to determine the gold-silver ratio with silver as currency. In addition, it also stipulates the minting of gold and silver coins, but this plan is purely permissive in nature, not compulsory.

Reuters, Washington, 21st – After President Roosevelt met with Senators King and Wheeler for a long time, it seems that a silver clause will be added to the authorities' currency inflation bill today. Senators King and Wheeler told people when they left the White House that the President had agreed to a silver clause, but the two senators were unwilling to announce the content of this clause. It is said that since the President has the right to stipulate the gold content in currency, he should also have the right to stipulate the silver content in currency, so that the ratio between gold and silver can be determined. Senators King and Wheeler have now returned to their congressional offices to draft their proposals.

President's Dictatorial Power May Not Be Used If Not Needed 83

National, Washington, 21st – When the British Prime Minister delivered his talk in Washington, it was learned from reliable sources that President Roosevelt's main wish at this time was only to increase the lending of the Federal Reserve Banks by 30 billion yuan. He will proceed with this matter as the first thing after Congress authorizes it. It is also heard that the President hopes that the situation created after the re-imposition of the gold ban can achieve the effect of self-regulating finance, and there will be no need to use the more radical provisions in the currency inflation bill. According to the report of the Ministry of Finance, although the transactions of various industries have increased sharply in recent days, the banks can still cope with it easily, and there is no great shortage of currency.

Hope to Quickly Pass Restrictions on Overproduction Through Congress 84

Havas, Washington, 22nd – President Roosevelt declared that the amendment to the rural relief bill proposed by Senator Thomas is indispensable in the economic recovery process. He hopes that Congress will pass it immediately, so that dictatorial power does not have to be used. The President also said that after the passage of this bill, the overproduction of agriculture can be controlled. If not, the benefits of the increase in agricultural product prices may be eliminated due to overproduction. As for the imbalance between the prices of agricultural products and industrial products, this bill cannot remedy it.

Futile Efforts to Balance Currency Prices in Anglo-American Negotiations 85

Havas, Washington, 22nd – It is learned that in a recent conversation between British Ambassador to the US, Lindsay, and US Secretary of State Hull, Hull firmly requested that the British government stabilize the pound sterling at a price of about $4.20 per pound. Lindsay replied that if the difference between the pound sterling and the US dollar were reduced, it would have an adverse impact on British commerce. Britain must acknowledge the cancellation of war debts before it can satisfy the United States on this point. Hull then said that the situation in the United States did not allow for the cancellation of war debts. In addition, Davis, the US representative to the disarmament conference in London, also made this kind of negotiation with the British Foreign Office. After these two negotiations, Roosevelt believed that it was futile to try to get the British government to stabilize the pound sterling and reduce its difference with the US dollar. He then decided to abandon the gold standard, hoping to create a situation to force countries to seek practical ways to restore currency balance. In this way, the depreciation of various currencies related to gold can be expected, and the stability of the world's general economy can be realized.

Hardliners Opposed to Modifying War Debts Change Their Attitudes 86

There is a new development in financial matters today. Several senators who have always stubbornly opposed modifying war debts are willing to consider it. Most senators generally agree to the provision allowing debtor countries to return silver, which is the first real indication of this trend. Senator Adams, who is known for opposing the modification of war debts, also stated today that he will offer an amendment to relax the amount of silver returned by debtor countries. (National Electric)

US Labor Circles Demand Increased Wages to Cope with Rising Prices 87

Havas, Washington, 22nd – The American Federation of Labor notified workers to fight together to demand increased wages. The abandonment of the gold standard and the implementation of currency inflation will inevitably raise prices, and increased wages are necessary to cope with it.

Reason Gradually Becomes Clear, Market Speculative Frenzy Slightly Declines 88

National, Washington, 21st – Today, the American people heard that the President hoped that it would not be necessary to use the more radical provisions in the currency inflation bill, and Prime Minister MacDonald arrived in New York. Former Treasury Secretary Mills suddenly arrived in Washington to lead the Republican Party to fight the currency inflation faction with all its strength, so as to avoid excessive actions in the monetary system. Because of these various influences, reason gradually became clear, and the speculative frenzy began to decline. Market prices also fell back. The fall in silver prices was almost as fierce as yesterday's soaring. The general impression is that the market has already been over-sold, so many people stopped doing new business.

National, Washington, 21st – The Republican Party's fight against currency inflation did not shock the government and the Democratic Party. Because even the Republican leaders believed that the bill would definitely pass. They knew that their opposition might not be effective, but they wanted the people to know the advantages and disadvantages of the various clauses of the bill. Former Treasury Secretary Mills' sudden arrival in Washington was completely unexpected. After he arrived in Washington, he immediately discussed everything with the key members of the House minority party and met with Senate Minority Leader Reed and House Minority Leader Snell for a long time. Afterwards, the party declared that it would not take organized obstructive action on the currency inflation bill, but would only insist on giving the minority party the opportunity to speak freely before the bill was put to a vote. It also admitted that the bill might be extended until after Prime Minister MacDonald left the United States before it was passed. However, the bill has been passed by the Finance Committee in the Senate today and sent out a favorable report. The government does not seem anxious about the bill being delayed. The government's attitude is also sufficient to verify that the US President does not want to use this bill as a negotiating weapon. He only wants to undertake the task of building a foundation for a successful meeting, which he has to undertake due to the situation.

British Public Opinion Tends to Be Moderate to Avoid Making Washington Talks Thorny 89

Havas, London, 22nd – After the United States abandoned the gold standard, the British public opinion's attitude of anger and agitation has greatly eased. It is very clear that people generally seek to avoid making Prime Minister MacDonald's mission to Washington thorny.

Expiration of the Turkish-Japanese Commercial Treaty 90

Electric Communication, Tokyo, 22nd – According to the announcement of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Japan-Turkey Provisional Commercial Agreement, which was established between Japan and Turkey in Showa 4 (1929), expired on May 6 of this year due to the notification of the Turkish government. However, the exchange of ratification of the formal commercial treaty between the Japanese and Turkish governments is currently underway.

Undercurrents Arise in Hitler's Cabinet 91

National Power Party Leader Issues Declaration

Havas, Berlin, 21st – Signs of unrest have arisen within Hitler's cabinet again. Last night, Hugenberg, the leader of the National Power Party and Minister of Agriculture and Commerce, issued a declaration in the party's newspapers, stating that in order to implement the (full-power) law, it must be on the condition that the central government, which is organized according to the current situation, continues to exist. Before this startling declaration was issued, Hugenberg had consulted with President Hindenburg, and their relationship became increasingly important. The German political atmosphere became heated due to Hugenberg's declaration. The National Power Party is deeply afraid that after the National Socialist Party conducts a revolution with nationalism, it will be followed by a revolution of socialism. As for Hitler, he is also afraid that the cabinet conflict will have serious effects. In addition, the German army completely obeys Hindenburg and is not affected by National Socialism. Therefore, Hitler wants to avoid the cabinet conflict by roundabout means and does not want Hindenburg to be involved.

Page 9

As an Internationally Popular Retaliation, Soviet Russia also Orders a Boycott of British Goods

London Russian Trade Representative Recalled, Hope for Release of British Technicians Suddenly Appears 92

Moscow, TASS, 22nd – In response to the recent British government's ban on Russian imports, the Soviet government has taken swift action. Today, People's Commissar for Foreign Trade, Rozengolts, issued an order regarding Anglo-Soviet trade, including the following measures:

(1) Prohibiting Soviet foreign trade organizations from issuing any orders to Britain and purchasing any goods.

(2) Prohibiting Soviet shipping organizations from hiring any British ships. (3) Establishing measures to restrict British goods passing through Soviet territory. (4) Ordering Soviet transportation and transshipment organizations to minimize the use of British ports.

The above measures are implemented in accordance with the decree passed by the Soviet Council of People's Commissars on October 20, 1930. They will remain in effect until Britain cancels the ban on Russian imports.

Moscow, TASS, 22nd – Soviet Foreign Trade Commissar Rozengolts has ordered the recall of the Soviet trade representative in London, Ozersky, and his two assistants. Ozersky and others will depart from London on April 24th and return directly to Moscow.

London, Reuters, 21st – The Soviet Russian trade delegation has issued a formal statement stating that no one is authorized to act on behalf of the delegation upon its departure from Britain and return to Russia. Therefore, there will effectively be no large number of new orders during this period. The head of the delegation, Vozhilsky, and his two assistants are scheduled to return to Moscow on Monday to consult with the Soviet Russian Foreign Trade Committee.

Moscow, TASS, 22nd – After Britain's ban on Russian imports, Anglo-Soviet trade will come to a standstill. The Soviet People's Commissariat for Water Transport today issued an order to impose higher taxes on British ships entering the country, to reflect the difference compared to the mutual benefit that existed when the Anglo-Russian trade agreement was in effect.

Moscow, Reuters, 21st – The lawyer of the imprisoned British engineer, Thornton, Browder, has today again petitioned the Central Executive Committee to overturn Thornton's and Macdonald's sentences, or reduce the sentence to deportation. It is expected that the Central Executive Committee will issue a decision soon. The current location of the two Britons in prison is not known for sure. It is generally believed to be in the Lubyanka prison. Foreigners in Moscow now believe that the two British technicians have hope of leaving Russian territory by the end of next week.

London, National News, 21st – Britain's ban on the sale of Russian goods and the Soviet Union's retaliatory actions have caused speculation here about their impact on the US recognition of Soviet Russia. Although some in the business community believe that the Russian market could greatly contribute to American foreign trade, many believe that the recent arrest of Vickers Company's British engineers by the Soviet Union will make the US more hesitant to resume diplomatic relations. Even the representatives of American businesses stationed in England share this view, saying that if the US restores diplomatic relations with Soviet Russia, American businesses may face the same treatment. The general public also believes that, regardless of whether the US recognizes Soviet Russia, if the Soviet Union can obtain credit from the US, some goods will be shifted to purchases from the US. Still others hope that the Soviet Union will realize that when Britain and Russia trade, the benefits to the Russians far outweigh those to the British, and will be able to change its attitude. The benefits gained by both countries in mutual trade can be seen in the following table:

| Year | British Goods to Russia (Pounds) | Russian Goods Sold to Britain (Pounds) | Britain's Intangible Exports to Russia (Pounds) |

|---|---|---|---|

| 1930 | 12,399,000 | 29,800,000 | 8,066,000 |

| 1931 | 15,018,000 | 32,179,000 | 7,000,000 |

| 1932 | 9,500,000 | 19,000,000 | 4,500,000 |

Furthermore, the recent Soviet Union's preparations to punish Germany's National Socialist Party's anti-Soviet policies are also being closely watched by American business representatives here. Several people have a deep impression that the trend of Soviet trade is uncertain.

After Our Troops Abandoned East of the Luan River 93

Special Dispatch from Beiping: Since the troops in eastern Luan retreated to the banks of the Luan River, the situation on the front line has changed. The Luan River area is crisscrossed by rivers and has a dangerous terrain. Our large army defended the area, and the enemy could not fly across it. Its importance is no less than the Great Wall. Therefore, although the war is becoming increasingly tense, the defense is very solid. The Japanese troops who invaded from the Lengkou area this time include the 16th Division, the 8th Division, and parts of the 6th Division, as well as the rebel troops of Li Jichun, Cheng Guorui, etc., totaling no less than 15,000 to 16,000 men, with a considerable momentum. Our troops fought separately and sacrificed greatly. Lulong and Funing were abandoned one after another. As of yesterday (the 17th), our troops had all retreated to the planned new positions. Japanese troops were found between Anshan and Shimen Station last night and contacted our cavalry Wang Division. Our Zhongshan armored train fired at the Japanese troops to provide cover and assistance. Zhugezhuang also had enemy troops arriving at the same time, attempting to destroy the tracks to cut off our army's return route. We received a report and sent troops to drive them away. The fighting between the two sides was fierce and has not stopped until this morning (the 18th). Cannon fire could be heard rumbling in Luanzhou city, very clearly, and the situation was extremely frightening. In order to threaten our troops, the Japanese army repeatedly sent large numbers of aircraft to bomb our army's positions. Today, Japanese aircraft flew to Luanzhou, Tangshan and other places to drop bombs. At the same time, Japanese aircraft were also found in Shixia Town, Miyun, Shunyi, and Tongzhou, which is very close to Beiping. The situation in North China is becoming more and more dangerous, and the people in the rear cannot help but feel terrified. The information obtained is recorded below.

(Japanese Aircraft Discovered in Tongzhou Dropping Three Bombs in Yanjiao)

(Tongzhou is Close to Beiping, Heavily Populated, and Commerce is Developed, Rejoicing)

Since the outbreak of war in Fengkou and other places, although the artillery fire on the front line has been fierce in recent days, the people in the rear have been peaceful and prosperous, coming and going, singing and dancing, maintaining a peaceful scene. The Tongzhou area was as calm as before, without any signs of alarm. Unexpectedly, the Japanese are ambitious and are advancing by leaps and bounds, and their acts of aggression have no end in sight. At 8:35 this morning, just as the general residents were waking up from a good dream, a buzzing sound suddenly shook their eardrums. An aircraft flew in the sky, like a dragonfly taking off. The fuselage was light gray, and the silver light was dazzling. It circled and did not leave. Soon, two more aircraft continued to arrive. Looking up, they saw the sun emblem painted on the wings of the aircraft. It was clearly a Japanese aircraft. As a result, the people of the whole city were greatly shocked and rushed to avoid it, and the situation became somewhat chaotic. The Japanese aircraft flew in the sky for a long time, reconnoitering for forty minutes before leaving. Earlier, the Japanese aircraft flew all the way from the Qinhuangdao area and reconnoitred in the territory of Sanhe County for a long time without dropping bombs. It then flew to Yanjiao near Sanhe and Tongzhou and dropped three bombs, causing slight damage. When it arrived at Tongzhou, it did not drop bombs, its intention being to intimidate and disrupt public morale. The flying height was about 3,000 meters. After leaving, it flew to Shunyi and Miyun, spreading leaflets with extremely absurd wording. It was already 9:30 in the morning. They all reconnoitred for a long time before leaving. For a time, the situation in various places became tense. As for Beiping, air defense facilities have been under planning for a long time, so the public morale is stable and there is no significant impact.

(Luan River East and West Banks Suffered Japanese Aircraft Bombing)

(Eight Japanese aircraft flew in formation to the east and west banks of the Luan River at about 8:00 this morning. They dropped more than forty bombs inside and outside the city, some of which were incendiary bombs. The places where they fell were filled with smoke and dust, and the fire was blazing, and the situation was extremely tragic. The people in the city took to the North-Ning Railway on foot, supporting the old and carrying the young, carrying packages, and fleeing west. Only one-tenth or two-tenths remained. The North-Ning eastbound passenger train could reach Luanzhou. Due to the congestion of refugees, the railway bureau could not allocate enough vehicles. It was specially dispatched a train from Tianjin and Tangshan stations to transport refugees. This morning, many Japanese aircraft also arrived in Tangshan to drop bombs and bomb, and many civilian houses were destroyed. The public was extremely terrified. Countless wealthy households fled to the Tianjin Concession or came to Beiping to seek refuge with relatives and friends. On the same day, at 9:30 this morning, eight Japanese aircraft flew to Shixia Town and dropped more than sixty heavy bombs, injuring more than twenty civilians. The number of buildings destroyed was also not small. Other stations on the North-Ning Line, such as Guye and Tuozi Tou, were also bombed by Japanese aircraft, so their purpose was to destroy our railways in an attempt to stop transportation. The poisonous means became more and more obvious, so the indignation of our people became more and more intense. (April 18th))

A Quick Sketch from Beiping to Zhangjiakou by Our Special Correspondent (Guo An) 94

Leaving the gray and decaying ancient city of Beiping, taking the dilapidated train of the PingSui Railway, and climbing towards the distant border. Wind and sand are the specialties of northern Mongolia, and the color of dead ashes fills everywhere. The vast yellow wilderness is lightly decorated with the scenery of spring green. To the west of the ancient city, there are ancient buildings with yellow bricks and green tiles, echoing with the low small houses.

The sun in the wind and sand casts a dim light. The carriages are crowded with soldiers and ragged old people, and there are also a few foreigners squeezed inside. In this air filled with different languages, breaths, and races, some are silent, some are yelling. I firmly occupy the only seat I have, constantly using my strength to resist the invading bodies.

After Shahe, we arrived at Changping. The mountains in the northwest stand tall, showing the natural danger of Nankou. Nankou Station is considered a station with more houses on this vast piece of land. The mountains in the southeast still retain the remnants of the fierce attack on Nankou by the Fengzhi-Lu Allied Forces in the 15th year of the Republic of China. I pay attention to this place where blood has been shed, but in the real environment, who dares to think about anything, especially the Japanese flag at the Great Wall Pass.

The train stopped at Nankou Station for half an hour, dropping a heavy locomotive, and at the same time hooking the locomotive to the tail of the train, preparing to pass through this dangerous mountain tunnel in Nankou. I stood on a guard car at the very front of the train, slowly watching the train pass through the tunnel. The train left Nankou a little bit and entered the valley. The steepest ridge of the stone mountain was covered as it crawled through this particularly slow train. The dilapidated walls of Juyongguan stood on the small mountain ridge in undulating sections. I quickly used my camera to take a close-up of the entrance. The train turned in different directions, climbing sometimes high and sometimes low.

I inadvertently discovered that the sleepers under the rails were either rotten or temporarily filled with debris. It was simply not easy to see any slightly newer sleepers. In this time of surrounding mountains and cliffs, I really felt that life in the train was too small. I didn't understand why this was the case. At this time, a worker watching the train was standing behind me. He said very playfully, "Sir, we are used to running and we are not afraid anymore."

"Why don't you replace the sleepers when they are so bad?" "Haha..." he laughed, but he didn't tell me the reason. In this way, I can only feel depressed! The train circled and went deeper and deeper. Looking down at the broken city of Juyongguan on the left, the stone tablet on the forehead of the first mountain tunnel was probably engraved with "Juyongguan Mountain Tunnel". The car entered the darkness for about two minutes, and then saw the light. At this time, the steep stone walls became more ferocious. When we reached the second cave, Yang Wulang's image was engraved on the left mountain wall, which the locals call "Wulang's Shadow". Unfortunately, my lens was too small to leave a trace. This tunnel was also very short. Further forward, it was simply entering the mountains. Soon we arrived at Qinglong Bridge. The bronze statue of Zhan Tianyou, the founder of the Pingsui Road, stood at the station, with a majestic face and a heroic posture, facing the stone wall and backing the mountain bay. I looked at it for a long time and couldn't help but feel respect.

The car stopped briefly and turned to the southwest. The locomotive turned its direction. Because this section was downhill, it was towed instead of pushed. Passing Badaling, the mountain shape became more dangerous. The dark cave lasted for several minutes. After seventy miles of mountain road, we finally passed safely. When we arrived at Kangzhuang, the station was still vast. The city was the rear general hospital, and the platform was covered with slogans. I vaguely remembered two sentences: "Society should be militarized, and the army should be socialized. Our army will not commit the slightest offense, so go and check." After the car passed Kangzhuang, the wind and sand covered the sun, and the desolate situation of northern Mongolia was fully expressed. The mountains in the distance, the sand in the near, the wind in the sky, and the earth underground rolled like tumbling on the vast wilderness. Here, you can't find the gentle spring breeze of the south of the Yangtze River and the intoxicating weather. Only yellow sand and white grass, and a earth-shattering gale sweeping across. When we arrived at Huailai, we saw the ancient city again, surrounded by mountains, and paved with bluestone like before. Mongolian ponies galloped with gray soldiers. Passing Shacheng, the setting sun trembled in the atmosphere of the wind on the west mountain. The scenery along the way was hungry. Xuanhua Prefecture is a large brick city with four sides, and the north also uses mountains as a barrier. Gray is more profound in the setting sun. □□□'s army is stationed in the city. I wandered around the platform for a long time, looking at the distant wilderness fire. In this vast place, plus the enemy's artillery fire and iron hooves, it is leaping forward more and more. What should we do? Arise, soldiers of the south of the Yangtze River! Enemy artillery fire is our club!

Chen Duxiu's Debate Summary (Continued) 95

Sentencing Set for the 26th of This Month

(The Defendants' Arguments)

After Attorneys Zhang, Peng, and Wu finished defending Chen Duxiu, it was 2:15 PM. The presiding judge announced a recess and adjourned the court, resuming the debate in the afternoon. At 4:00 PM, the court session continued, and the audience seats were even more crowded than in the morning. After the court clerk announced the resumption of the session, each defendant was called upon to present their defense, with their attorneys also presenting arguments on their behalf. The arguments of the defendants and the lawyers' defense speeches are summarized below:

(Peng Shuzhi) Peng Daoshu's reasons for opposing the Kuomintang and the National Government were as follows: (1) The National Government has failed to abolish all unequal treaties. Imperialists still control customs, concessions have not been recovered, consular jurisdiction has not been revoked, and imperialist armies rampage at will. Japan has even occupied the four northeastern provinces, and Shanghai has been occupied once. Therefore, imperialism must be overthrown. (2) The warlords in various provinces have engaged in years of internal warfare, causing suffering to the people, bankruptcy in rural areas, and economic decline in cities. Therefore, the warlords must be disarmed. (3) The people lack freedom, and capitalists are unpatriotic. Currently, the donations in various regions are all contributed by ordinary people, while capitalists and landlords do not contribute a penny. Only farmers and workers possess revolutionary spirit. Based on the above facts and reasons, upholding the interests of the people is not treason. If the court upholds the law, it should declare him innocent.

Attorney Zhang Shizhao added in his defense that it was largely the same as his defense for Chen Duxiu, with the following additions: (1) The defendant admitted to being a communist and opposing the National Government, but not with the intention of implementing communism. It was because the National Government could not implement the Three Principles of the People. There is no provision in the law that makes being a communist a crime, so the defendant's crime cannot be established. (2) The defendant's opposition to the Kuomintang did not compare the Three Principles of the People with communism, and the reason for opposing the Kuomintang was that it could not implement the Three Principles of the People. Article 2, Section 2 of the Emergency Law for the Punishment of Offenses Against the Republic of China refers to propagating doctrines incompatible with the Three Principles of the People, so it cannot be applied. (3) Furthermore, factually speaking, Peng did not engage in propaganda work. The publications he printed, "Spark" and "Campus Life," were in very small quantities, and the government prohibited their circulation. Only his friends who believed in communism saw them, so they only had ideas and did not develop them. Even if they were developed, it was very limited, far from what is regulated by the Emergency Law for the Punishment of Offenses Against the Republic of China, so it cannot be applied. The reasons stated by the defendant are not based on the standpoint of communism at all, but rather because of his fervent patriotism, and it could even be said that he is concerned about protecting the Kuomintang. It is illegal to impose a sentence without a law, so please declare the defendant innocent.

Attorney Peng Wangye argued that the defendant's opposition to the Kuomintang and the National Government did not endanger the Republic of China. If the nation, government, and party are not regarded as a trinity or a duality, then it cannot be said to endanger the Republic of China. Furthermore, the government is progressive and infinitely progressive. The Kuomintang's achievements can be considered very good in some aspects, while unsatisfactory in others. It cannot be said that someone is committing a crime simply because they criticize. As for the part about written propaganda, because it was prohibited by the government, it did not achieve its purpose and can only be regarded as an attempted crime. The Emergency Law for the Punishment of Offenses Against the Republic of China cannot be applied.

Attorney Wu Zhiping argued that the defendant's publications were not circulated, so there was no propaganda. The prosecutor's accusations cannot be applied. Furthermore, studying academics is not prohibited by law, so he should be declared innocent. At this point, Chen Duxiu and Peng Shuzhi both stood up to add a statement that Attorney Zhang's defense, based on his personal observations and criticisms presented to the court, were entirely his personal opinions and were not solicited from them, nor did they need to be solicited. Their political views should not be based on Attorney Zhang's defense but should be based on their own documents.

Wang Wu Wang Wu continued to argue that his previous crime had already been judged and was unrelated to this case. He suffered from severe illnesses such as lung, stomach, and foot diseases. When he was released on bail on October 5th, his family had already left Shanghai because they had run out of money, instructing him to return home immediately after his release. Because he was poor and desperate, he had no choice but to meet Xie Shaoshan. Xie Shaoshan agreed to lend him money and take him to his home. He talked to Xie’s wife, who told him to rest and recover. He was arrested shortly thereafter. Xie is not a defendant, which shows that he was acting as a government informant with the intention of framing him. However, he did not take any action. Regarding the Standing Committee matter, elections must have a basis, but there is no basis now, which shows that it is not accurate. The meeting matter is also not true. Witnesses from the Shanghai Public Security Bureau said it seemed like a meeting, with each person having a pen and notebook. However, no physical evidence has been presented now. Moreover, only Western detectives were present during the arrest, and no personnel from the Public Security Bureau were present. Now, it is only based on Xie Shaoshan's words, which cannot be considered. Xie wants to become an official, so he does not hesitate to frame others. Chen Duxiu and Peng Shuzhi have both testified that he is not a member of the Standing Committee. He was extremely ill when he came out of prison, so how could he do anything? Therefore, saying that he was holding a meeting is as ridiculous as saying that a sick person won a 10,000-meter race championship.

Attorney Peng Wangye argued that the defendant joined the Communist Party in the fourteenth year of the Republic and was arrested in Shanghai by the Garrison Command in the twentieth year of the Republic, sentenced to six years in prison. During the amnesty, the sentence was reduced to four years. He was released on bail on October 5th of last year and was arrested again on the 15th. He had no activities during the ten days of his bail. Factually speaking, prisoners who can obtain bail must have very serious illnesses that prison doctors cannot treat. Since the defendant had a serious illness, how could he engage in political activities? Furthermore, being elected to the Standing Committee is definitely impossible. The defendant went to Xie Shaoshan's house to borrow money, and he was arrested while talking to Xie’s wife, which proves that he did not participate in the meeting. Moreover, the Public Security Bureau said that everyone had a pen and notebook during the meeting, but there are no such items in the case now. Xie Shaoshan once testified that all five members of the Standing Committee were arrested, and no one escaped. Therefore, no one would have destroyed the evidence after the arrest. Why can't the Public Security Bureau provide the evidence? This shows that it cannot be used as a reference. As for the Standing Committee matter, if he was elected before going to prison, then it has already been judged. If it is said that he was elected in prison, then this is definitely impossible. As for saying that he was elected after being released from prison, it has already been stated that he was too ill to participate in political activities, which is even more unreasonable.

Pu Yifan Pu argued that when he was arrested, he was ordered to find Zeng Shengwei, the former general manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Li Weihou, who is currently detained in prison. The court only needs to investigate to understand. He has never joined a political party. He is very busy at the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and has no time to participate in political activities. This can be verified by the attendance book of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. As for the Standing Committee matter, he does not understand it at all. Chen and Peng said that the alternate was Pu Yifang, a Sichuan native, who is completely unrelated to him. To take a step back, if it is said that he is a member of the Communist Party, how could he be called Pu Yifan in the party and also be called Pu Yifan at the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company? Furthermore, in terms of propaganda, he edited the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Monthly. The court can check if there are any political texts or propaganda texts. As for the box found in his residence, the box was deposited by his friend Su Shaoqing. The box has his name card on it. When the police arrested him, they asked him for his address, and he frankly told them. If he had reactionary documents, how could he have given them his address? Moreover, the police did not handle the search of the box in accordance with the law, which is even more inappropriate. After he was arrested, the personal mental and material losses are needless to say, and his elderly mother has gone blind from crying because of this. His wife and children have nothing to eat. Please declare him innocent.

Attorney Liu Zuwang argued: (1) There must be proof of the meeting. Lu Wenhu of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau said that when they were arrested, they looked like they were holding a meeting. Such uncertain and speculative statements cannot be used as evidence. Moreover, there are no pens or notebooks, which is even more baseless. (2) There is also no proof of the alternate Standing Committee matter. It cannot be used as evidence based solely on Xie Shaoshan's words. The defendant works for the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, which is a government agency. How could it accommodate a communist Standing Committee member? Pu Yifan and Pu Yifang sound the same, which must be a misrepresentation. (3) As for the books, if the defendant were guilty, he would not have given his address. Moreover, when the search was conducted, Chen Julai and Wang Xiaochun were waiting for the defendant to return home. Chen was released at the time because he was not involved, and Wang was also released later. As for the box, it was deposited by Su Shaoqing, and there are Su's personal letters and name cards in the box, which shows that it is not the defendant's. Even if, to take a step back, it were the defendant's, all reactionary books cannot be considered crimes according to Interpretation No. 502 of the Judicial Yuan. Therefore, please declare the defendant innocent.

Wang Ziping Wang argued that after being expelled, he did not join the Trotskyists. He printed "Spark" because he could not make a living, and he started printing from the eighth issue. If he were a Trotskyist, he should have started printing from the first issue. He had been unemployed for a long time and had repeatedly applied for jobs, but he was not hired due to the large number of applicants. He had no choice but to go into printing. Moreover, the printing work was not important. Xie Shaoshan brought it every time, and he took it away after printing. He was only solving his livelihood problem.

Attorney Peng Wangye argued that the defendant was engaged in printing solely due to the pressure of making a living. Although the defendant had once joined the Communist Party, he cannot be regarded as an accomplice in a crime. In terms of the subjective aspect, there should be contact with the principal offender. In terms of the objective aspect, the result should be examined. The defendant is not related to Chen Duxiu and others and only copied for them when hired. Furthermore, propaganda relies on words. If Xie Shaoshan does not bring the manuscript, he cannot print it. Therefore, he cannot be considered an accomplice and should be found not guilty.

Attorney Jiang Haoshi made a joint statement on behalf of all defendants: (1) Xie Shaoshan's confession in the police station cannot be adopted as evidence. Xie is an important figure in the Communist Party, but he is not facing charges himself. He made random confessions in order to avoid charges, so it cannot be adopted. (2) There is no evidence of any kind. The prosecutor's accusation is based entirely on speculation and cannot be adopted. As for Wang Ziping, although he once joined the Communist Party, the law does not apply retroactively. He did not join the Trotskyists after being expelled. He engaged in printing solely for the sake of bread. The government and society should be responsible for youth unemployment. The defendant is not responsible for the crime.

He Afang He argued that Xie Shaoshan told him to print, and he only printed one issue. He was arrested before it was finished. Printing is not a crime because someone writes the articles, someone edits them, and someone distributes them after printing. They should be responsible. For example, making a handgun, the handgun can kill people, but it cannot be said that the maker of the handgun is committing a crime. He went to print entirely for the sake of twenty yuan a month, and it did not conflict with his original occupation as a coppersmith.

Attorney Wu Zhiping argued that the defendant is not responsible. He has already explained that he only printed once and was arrested before it was finished. The Emergency Law for the Punishment of Offenses Against the Republic of China does not have any provisions for this situation. According to Article 30, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law, he is only guilty of an attempted crime and should not be punished.

Attorney Peng Wangye argued that although the defendant was engaged in printing, he cannot be immediately considered to have joined the Trotskyists because there is no evidence and it is only based on imagination, which cannot be used as evidence.

Wang Zhaoqun Wang argued: (1) Xie Shaoshan confessed that his home was a communist organization. He and I were arrested at the same time. According to the law, he should be a defendant along with us. He has other purposes, so he intentionally harmed people. Although I live in Xie's house, there is no other evidence to say that I am a communist organization. (2) There is no evidence of any kind, so it cannot constitute a crime. If the court protects the law, it should declare him innocent.

Attorney Peng Wangye argued that the prosecutor said that Xie's home was a communist organization, and if the defendant had no relationship, he would not be allowed to live in it. This is an inaccurate conclusion based on an inaccurate premise.

Attorney Jiang Haoshi argued that Lu Wenhu of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau said that the defendant was standing at the window when they were arrested, which shows that he did not participate in the meeting. Moreover, the Western detective Gode never said anything about a meeting, which shows that Lu Wenhu's words are unreliable.

Guo Jinghao Guo argued that if he were a communist, why would there be no evidence found in his home? Furthermore, why wasn't the school registration form presented at the Second Branch of the Shanghai Higher Court, the Public Security Bureau, and the Jiangsu Higher Court? It was only presented now, which shows that it was fabricated. The form says that he joined the party in Changsha in 1925. At that time, he was still studying in elementary school in his hometown and had never been to Changsha. The form also says that he joined the Trotskyists in Shanghai in the nineteenth year of the Republic. It should be known that he only arrived in Shanghai at the end of the nineteenth year of the Republic.

Attorney Wu Zhiping argued that the defendant is Peng Shuzhi's younger brother. It cannot be said that the younger brother is also a communist simply because the older brother is a communist. There must be direct evidence of a crime. Furthermore, the origin of the registration form cannot be explained even by the staff of the Public Security Bureau, which shows that it is not a legitimate basis.

Attorney Peng Wangye argued that the Public Security Bureau, because there was no evidence after the defendant was arrested, fabricated the registration form to frame the defendant for fear that he would demand compensation.

Attorney Jiang Haoshi argued that the court should pay attention to the fact that there is no other evidence of the defendant's crime. There is only a registration form with no origin.

Liang Youguang Liang argued that he is not a communist at all, and the court also has no evidence. Please declare him innocent immediately.

Attorney Jiang Haoshi argued that the defendant came to Shanghai to find his younger brother. It is not surprising that he escaped from the window when he was arrested. There are many robbery cases and kidnappers in Shanghai. Seeing many people with guns entering in the middle of the night, anyone who would not want to escape in this situation, I say he must not be human. Furthermore, Xie Shaoshan confessed that he was a Guangxi inspector, which is also baseless. If saying that someone came from Guangxi means that they are a Guangxi inspector, then someone who went from Nanjing to Shanghai would be a Nanjing inspector.

When Wang Jiantang Wang argued, he stuttered and could not argue. Only his explanation of the box was heard. In conclusion, he said, "Please, judges, let me go home," causing laughter throughout the courtroom.

Attorney Jiang Haoshi argued that this kind of person is neither qualified for research nor qualified for work. What would the Communist Party want with this kind of person? If the small piece of paper that was found has the character "Chen" on it, it is said to be Chen Duxiu, which is too illogical. Perhaps the police could not catch Wang Boping, so they caught a Wang Jiantang to shirk their responsibility.

Declaration of the End of Debate 96

At this point, it was 6:35 PM. All defendants and defense attorneys had completed their arguments. The presiding judge asked each defendant again if they had anything else to say. Except for Wang Jiantang, who stuttered, saying, "Let me go home," the rest had nothing to say. The presiding judge then declared the end of the debate, and the sentencing was set for the afternoon of the 26th of this month (Central News Agency).

Songjiang 97

Kidnapping of Children Occurred Outside the North Gate. Zhang Menglin and Zhang Pulin, two brothers living in Maojia Village, about three miles outside the North Gate, make a living by farming and live diligently. On the night of the eleventh day of the first month of the lunar calendar, a gang of bandits suddenly came, ransacked the village, and kidnapped two children named Disheng, aged twelve, and Jinfa, aged six, before leaving. Initially, out of eagerness to rescue them, they dared not report to the authorities. Now, after many days with no news, they have reported to the Public Security Bureau for investigation and rescue.

Nanhui 98

Execution of a Thief

Zhang Alin, a native of Chongming, colluded with Lu Arong, Lu Awen, Chen Shengting, Xue Gengsheng, a tailor from Chaoyang, Song Shuitao, and others to rob the property of Lu Zhangsheng, a farmer in Yutan Township, Third District, in February. Only one suspect was captured afterwards. He was brought to the county and confessed to the joint robbery without denying it. The county proposed a death sentence and reported it to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for approval. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, the suspect was brought out, his identity was verified, he was tied up, taken to the execution ground, and executed by firing squad to serve as a warning.

Zhang Tianshi Comes South to Handle Registration of 法師 99

Local News

Reduction of Working Hours Implemented by Chinese-Owned Cotton Mills in the City Yesterday 104

The Municipal Government Continued Deliberating on Relief Measures Yesterday Morning

The Cotton Mill Association Designated Representatives to Petition in the Capital

All Other Cities Besides Tianjin Have Already Implemented the Measures

After the National Chinese Cotton Mill Association resolved on measures to reduce working hours, all Chinese-owned cotton mills in the city, including Hengfeng and Shenxin, suspended operations yesterday. The municipal government and other agencies reconvened at 10:00 a.m. yesterday to discuss relief measures. Details are recorded below: (All Factories Suspended Operations) The Cotton Mill Association's resolution to reduce working hours was implemented yesterday, with all day and night shifts suspended every Saturday and Sunday, or a 23% reduction in working hours. As for the city's Chinese-owned cotton mills, totaling 28, including Hengfeng, except for the three mills including Yongyu that were already shut down, and Jingwei, which is a waste cotton mill and therefore operates as usual, the remaining mills including Shenxin have all decided to suspend operations on Saturday and Sunday day and night shifts every week. Yesterday was Saturday, and all factories were completely shut down. Notices from the Cotton Mill Association were posted at the gates of all factories, stating that work would resume on Monday.

(Inspection of Various Factories) The General Meeting of the Cotton Mill Association, for the matter of reducing working hours, appointed the city's supervisory committee members Huang Shoumin, Li Shengbo, and Xue Chunsheng, three individuals to specifically oversee the reduction of working hours in various factories. Yesterday was the first Saturday of the reduction in working hours. At 7:00 a.m., supervisory committee member Xue Chunsheng and two others went by car to inspect various Chinese-owned cotton mills to see if any were violating the resolution. They returned around 1:00 p.m., and it was found that all factories were uniformly complying, the workers were scattered at home, and the order was very good.

(Continued Deliberation by the Municipal Government) At 10:00 a.m. yesterday, the municipal government reconvened both labor and management representatives, as well as figures from the banking community, in the conference room on the third floor of the municipal government, to continue discussing relief measures. Those present included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Director Liu Yinbo of the Ministry of Industry, Wu Zhongheng representing the Central Party Headquarters, Jiang Huaisu representing the Municipal Party Headquarters, Wu Hengru, Wang Ze, Qin Hongji of the Social Affairs Bureau, Nie Lusheng, Zhang Zemin, Guo Shun representing the Chinese cotton mills, Lu Jingshi representing the labor community, and Chen Jianan, Wu Yunzhai, Xu Xinliu, Lin Kanghou, and Qin Xieqing representing the banking community. Mayor Wu presided over the meeting, which adjourned at 12:00 noon. According to Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, who spoke to a reporter from the New Sound News Agency after the meeting, the meeting concluded that the disastrous decline of the cotton mill industry was a fundamental problem of emerging industry, and that reducing working hours was merely a stopgap measure. In order to seek fundamental relief, it was decided that representatives should be dispatched from the cotton mill industry to the capital to discuss relief measures with the relevant financial and industrial departments, and to provide subsidies or reduce burdens within a possible range.

(Conditions in Various Ports) This reduction in working hours was decided by the General Meeting of the Chinese Cotton Mill Association, which convened representatives from all factories in Tianjin, Hankou, Wuxi, and Shanghai. Therefore, this reduction in working hours concerns all Chinese-owned cotton mills nationwide, not limited to Shanghai alone. Factories in Wuxi, Hankou, and other inland areas also uniformly implemented the resolution yesterday morning. In Wuxi, the method of reducing working hours by 23% was mostly used. However, the Tianjin area, due to the tense war situation, has reported to Shanghai by telegram, fearing that it would affect public order, and was unable to implement the measure as scheduled yesterday. It has been agreed that the measure will be implemented before May 21, to await a slight easing of the situation. Currently, factories are reducing working hours and stopping spindles in tandem, with 23% as the standard.

(Number of Working Hour Reductions) According to a survey report from the National Chinese Cotton Mill Association, the total number of working hour reductions is as follows: there are a total of 82 Chinese-owned cotton mills nationwide, of which 60 are members of the association. In Shanghai, there are 8 mills in total, of which 26 are members of the association, with 1,117,000 yarn spindles and 7,800 looms. Outside of Shanghai, there are 54 mills, of which 34 are members of the association, with 1,134,000 yarn spindles and 11,100 looms. In total, the reduction in working hours involves 2,250,000 yarn spindles and 19,000 looms.

(Record Filing for Working Hour Reductions) After resolving to reduce working hours, the Chinese Cotton Mill Association immediately submitted a report to the central government for record filing, stating briefly: "Since 1928, the world's economic situation has been declining, and all countries are suffering from overproduction, using the method of dumping to expand overseas markets. Our country has the lightest tariffs, and has become the end of the dumping chain. Since the massive floods of the 20th year of the Republic, followed by the Japanese invasion of Jehol and Shanghai, the rural economy has been on the verge of bankruptcy, financial resources have been tightening daily, purchasing power has been weak, and demand has been greatly reduced. Japanese factories in China are further dumping yarn and cloth at reduced prices, and the outlets for Chinese factories' yarn and cloth have been greatly reduced. Since the beginning of this year, the situation has been declining daily, ultimately causing yarn and cloth prices to reach the lowest figures since the first year of the Republic, while the stock of yarn and cloth in various places has reached an unprecedentedly large volume. At a time of extremely tight finances and high interest rates, manufacturers are almost all in a precarious situation. The association's factories, knowing that they should strive to invigorate themselves and recover from the decline, are unable to sell their products, even at extremely low prices. Raw material, cotton, is in short supply domestically, and its price does not decline in equal proportion to yarn and cloth. The use of foreign cotton is also costly due to expensive exchange rates. Comparing the lowest prices of yarn and cotton in March of this year with the entire year of the 19th year of the Republic, yarn has fallen by 24 taels, while cotton has risen by 3 taels. Therefore, there is not only no room for remedy between raw materials and products, but the business is becoming increasingly unfavorable. Secondly, we are starting from the opening and payment aspects, in order to slightly reduce costs. If you want to reduce the opening and payment, there are only two ways: reduce expenses and increase production. Looking back at the past three to five years, the wages of employees have gradually increased. It is already difficult not to increase them, how can we dare to reduce them again? As for increasing production, it was originally the only method for the national relief industry in recent times, but in terms of the current state of our country's factories, work has already been neglected, and maintaining the status quo is already challenging. Seeking to increase production is really like a dream. Therefore, rationalization has been promoted in various countries, but we still have no way to implement it. Speaking of this, it is really heartbreaking. The textile industry is in this kind of difficult and dangerous situation, not just overnight. The financial resources of the factories are weak, and they have long been exhausted and difficult to support. However, because the cotton industry is so important to the national economy and the people's livelihood, we have to reluctantly maintain it, waiting for a slight improvement in the timing. Since last winter, the situation has become increasingly worse, and there is no hope of a turnaround in the foreseeable future. Losses have been increasing, and it has become difficult to maintain operations. Under duress, a meeting of various factories was convened on April 10. Everyone agreed that foreign aggression and domestic worries are becoming increasingly serious. If there is no emergency relief, we will all perish together. After unanimous discussion by the factory representatives, it was resolved that all factories would uniformly implement the reduction of working hours from April 22 to May 21, and all factories would completely shut down day and night every Saturday and Sunday, in order to reduce production and maintain survival, etc. The association has already notified various factories to implement the measures on schedule. The association's resolution to reduce working hours is really a struggle for survival, seeking active relief. Otherwise, the products will accumulate daily and cannot be sold, and almost the entire industry will inevitably collapse. Not only will the factories be on the verge of bankruptcy, but the impact on the social economy will be beyond comparison with the current reduction in working hours. How should we properly plan for relief in the future? Your department cares about industry and must respond to the manufacturers' eager expectations."

(Representatives Going to the Capital) According to the Central News Agency, the meeting decided that the Cotton Mill Association would send representatives to the capital to appeal for relief. The municipal government will also send a telegram to the capital to appeal. The Cotton Mill Association designated Rong Zongjing, Guo Shun, and Nie Lusheng as representatives. Rong has already taken the express train attached to a flower car to the capital at 10:00 a.m. yesterday. Guo and Nie are scheduled to depart tomorrow (Monday). According to Nie Lusheng, who spoke to reporters yesterday, the Cotton Mill Association, in order to seek fundamental relief, has decided to petition the authorities. A petition has been drafted, stating the dumping of foreign goods, the impact on Chinese yarn, and the resulting business downturn, and requesting several points, the main idea being to reduce burdens or provide subsidies and rewards.

Case of Factory Inspection Rights 105

Regarding the case of the government sending personnel to investigate the Public Concession's attempt to seize our factory inspection rights, Mayor Wu of our city issued a solemn statement the day before yesterday, and the Municipal Party Headquarters also issued a declaration the day before yesterday. The central government is paying unusual attention to this matter because it concerns our country's labor administration rights, and will send personnel to Shanghai to investigate the truth of the case and discuss countermeasures.

Expression by the Citizens' Federation 106

The First Special District Citizens' Federation sent a letter to the Public Works Department, stating: "To the Honorable Directors, we find that our country's Factory Law and Factory Inspection Law have been promulgated and implemented. If there is no obstruction from extraterritorial forces, they will surely be implemented soon. The core of these factory laws and regulations is to uphold (humanitarianism), so they pay special attention to the health and safety of workers, and are based on the most advanced legal concepts in the world. According to the execution, there is practically no problem, and as a national law, there is practically no exception in legal principle. We do not know why the previous board of directors of your bureau, due to what background, misinterpreted the Yangjingbang Land Regulations and proposed to the current ratepayers' Westerners meeting to amend Article 34 of the appendices, adding an item on factory licensing, and still falsely claiming (humanitarianism) to confuse the public. Our country's factory laws and regulations, which are implemented within our country's territory, are indisputable in legal principle. The agreement or disagreement of the ratepayers within this district on this case is extraneous, and legally cannot have any effect. Our federation need not make any representations to your bureau, but from your bureau's standpoint, we feel that this amendment has raised an extremely serious and complex problem, and we must plan ahead to avoid future disputes, and make the following statements. The foundation of your bureau is built on the Yangjingbang Land Regulations. After the addition of the Chinese Director case in the 14th year of the Republic, its nature fundamentally changed. To put it bluntly, your bureau not only in fact, but also in legal principle, must abide by the opinions of all or the majority of the ratepayers in the district. Any partiality is discrimination, which would render its foundation unsound. Now, with regard to the amendment of the appendices, two points of view have arisen among the ratepayers: (disagreement) and (agreement). If your bureau recognizes its position and is free from misguidance, or has no subjective prejudice, it is truly like a woman between two mothers-in-law, difficult to navigate on both sides. As the saying goes, (There is nothing wrong with the world, but mediocre people disturb themselves.) This is what it means. Therefore, our federation is brainstorming and has no choice but to find a way to eliminate this case. However, observing your bureau's past behavior, we cannot help but speak out. It seems that the amendment is inevitable. The former General Director's radio broadcast, the speeches proposing the amendment, the intelligence office's propaganda, the public works department's supply and transportation, and the fact that it was carried out after the Chinese ratepayers had disagreed with the case, all seem to disregard the opinions of the ratepayers who account for more than 95% of the population and pay more than 55% of the taxes, and to forget their great contribution to maintaining the progress of municipal administration. This is tantamount to implying that the aforementioned ratepayers need not fulfill their obligations. Out of deep love, we cannot help but speak frankly, and respectfully ask for your understanding, so as to avoid unnecessary disputes. We are at the height of our hopes." Respectfully addressed to the Board of Directors of the Shanghai Public Concession.

As for the Sino-Belgian treaty, it was signed into a new treaty of equality on October 22 of the 17th year of the Republic, when Juye Moreau last served as the envoy to China, and it was renewed for three years after its expiration on October 22 last year, so there is no need to amend it at this time. The claim that the 1865 Sino-Belgian treaty will be amended is actually ignorance of the history of the Sino-Belgian treaty. The old treaty of 1865 was abolished four years ago. The new treaty signed in the 17th year of the Republic recognized the abandonment of consular jurisdiction, but stated that it must be implemented when all the countries concerned agree.
