Free Talk

The Will of Heaven 209

— Cao Juren

Wearing cotton clothes in April, the weather is really a bit strange. The poem "First Month" says: (In the first month (the month of positive yang), now in April, frost is heavy, my heart is sad.) Strange weather existed in ancient times, we ourselves cannot help but (my heart is sad).

When the Yuan army attacked Hangzhou, they set up tents on the beach of the Qiantang River. The Song people thought that heaven was destroying the Suo barbarians, and that this would solve everything. Who knew that the river tide would not arrive for three days, and the Yuan soldiers attacked Hangzhou. There is a great deal of the will of heaven in this. This year, the wind in Luoyang is particularly strong, making it inconvenient even to practice flying, so it is necessary to lead the team back south to Hangzhou. (See the newspapers of April 21) It is true that the wind makes it inconvenient to practice flying; when children fly kites in the spring, if the wind is too strong, they have to take in the kite to avoid breaking the string. Everyone understands this basic knowledge. The wind is strong in Luoyang, there must be the will of heaven in this! However, the will of heaven is unpredictable. The wind is strong in Luoyang, and our planes have already flown back to Hangzhou; if a Japanese plane tries to fly over, it will be blown down, isn't this the boundless happiness of the Republic of China!

Some people, based on Liu Bowen's Shao Bing Song, say: (The Xuantong Emperor will still have thirty-six years of rule.) It can be seen that the fall of Beiping and Tianjin was originally within the will of heaven. The sage Hu told us to wait for fifty years, the sage revealed the secrets of heaven to save all living beings, his grace is limitless. We should quickly lie down in the pit, each person getting a pipe, facing each other under a lamp, so as not to disappoint the good intentions of the sage Hu. If we don't get a pipe, but play golf, dance and drink champagne, and bet on greyhounds and jai alai, that is also a kind of rest, and there is no reason to object. Fifty years later, the will of heaven will turn, we will leap out of the pit, planes will fly out of Hangzhou; the sun will be bright and the wind clear, the pipes will be invincible, the kite strings will never break, and China will be saved.

Therefore, the other side of the will of heaven in the fall of Tianjin is the Eastern Renaissance. The fall of Constantinople led to the westward movement of culture, and the fall of Beiping led to the southward movement of (culture). Haven't you seen that the masters of the Renaissance have already been born! Alas, the principle of prosperity and decline, although it is said to be human affairs, is it not the will of heaven!

Introducing Renard and His "Carrot Top" 210

— Lie Wen

We have only selected Renard's "Carrot Top" from the vast sea of modern literary masterpieces, and there is no other reason, only because it is a long novel that can be taken apart, composed of several short stories, which is easier to edit and easier to read. Although Renard has a considerable position in the history of world literature, it seems that few people in China know about him. Here I must write a few words to introduce him: Renard's name in Western languages is JULES RENARD, born in CHALONS in the M A Y E N N E province of northwestern France in 1864, and died very early, enjoying less than fifty years of life. But in this short life, his literary achievements were already amazing; he was elected as one of the ten members of the famous Goncourt Academy (A C A D E M I E G O N C O U R T).

From 1888, he successively published novels such as "Crime de Village," "Sou rire Spin ces," and "Le Cornifle ur." In 1894, "Poil de Carotte" (Carrot Top) was published, and he became famous immediately. This novel was later adapted into a play, which achieved great success on the stage. "Carrot Top" in France, like Ah Q in China, has become a well-known typical character. "Carrot Top" is a somewhat silly, unfortunate child who grows up in a very bad family and suffers from heavy oppression; a biased mother abuses him; a selfish father always ignores him; and cunning older brothers and sisters also take advantage of the environment to bully him. Living his days in this kind of atmosphere, Carrot Top gradually becomes cunning, lazy, and cruel. There are no particularly surprising plots in this book; Renard gives us a series of consecutive cartoons with skilled brushstrokes. Every character in the picture has undergone accurate observation and careful dissection, and many scams or base places in each person's daily life that are not easily seen are shown on paper. Such cartoons not only give people a sense of emotion, but also allow attentive readers to experience a kind of calm ridicule everywhere. The famous historian Gustave Lanson said that this is an unprecedented masterpiece of originality, which is not an overstatement.

Because in recent years, many of the foreign literary works translated in China are either translated incorrectly or are so difficult to understand, that most readers tend to many easily digestible (creations), and they turn away from Western masterpieces of more value. This magazine intends to publish a few faithful and clear translations within the possible scope, and honestly do some introductory work. The translation of (Carrot Top) can also be said to be our first attempt.

Hometown Miscellany 211

— Mu Shiying

(4) Uncle Jun

Uncle Jun is a distant cousin, I don't see him very often; in my impression, he is such a kind middle-aged man, always stroking my hair, asking me if I have finished reading the Classic of Filial Piety. It was the year I was nine years old that he ran to my house in great despair, talked to my father, and then left, returning to Ningbo. When I went back eight years ago, I saw him, and he still asked if my dad was well, if my mom was well, if my younger brothers and sisters were well, and he bought a lot of food for me. At that time, he was still such an elegant and polite gentleman. Later, every year when people from the countryside came up, I always heard people say that he had sold this and sold that. From people's mouths, I learned that he had already sold his daughter and sold his family's graveyard, and had become a pauper who didn't even have a long coat; from people's mouths, I learned that last winter he slept on straw and almost froze to death there; from people's mouths, I learned that he had only a wife who smoked opium, a son who smoked opium, and his own opium-smoking mouth, a thin shadow. Once, someone mentioned his youngest son, Zhongshou, my cousin: (Zhongshou is very pitiful, neither his mom likes him, nor his dad likes him, every day he goes to the town, takes a broken huqin, sings and plays, asking people for a few coins to make a living. That day, I don't know how he ran to Mu Village, stood in front of Aunt Wuling's house singing ditties and asking for money. As soon as Aunt Wuling saw him, she told him not to play anymore, gave him a yuan, but he didn't even take the money, covered his face and left, and hasn't been seen since, I don't know where he ran off to...) Hearing these words, that kind middle-aged man floated back into my memory, along with a sad face that no longer smiled slightly, asking me if I had finished reading the Classic of Filial Piety. Why? Why would such a good person have such a bad fate? That day, after sweeping the tombs of my great-grandfather and great-great-grandfather, I saw him sitting alone in the main room, everyone else was playing cards in the room, ignoring him. They hid everything, not even giving him a teacup or a water pipe, guarding him like a thief. I felt sorry for him, went inside to pour a cup of tea, took a cigarette, and just as I was about to go to him, my aunt pulled me back and said; (Don't go, he has lice on him). But I still went and gave him the cigarette and tea. He smoked the cigarette without saying a word, his head lowered, not daring to look at me. He sat there very awkwardly, his hair was so long that it hung over his shoulders, a pair of eyes like those of a neurasthenic patient, staring at the ground, tucking his feet under the chair. Because he was wearing a pair of heel-less shoes, he was afraid I would see them. Several times he put his arms on the table, and then hurriedly pulled them back, because there was a hole in his arm, and the cuffs were gone. His face was full of sadness, and the flesh had hung down, he was so haggard!

I sat with him until evening, and he only said one sentence: (Shanghai is probably very different from before, right? I haven't been there for more than ten years). He swallowed a sigh.

When it was time for dinner, only I accompanied him, everyone else avoided him, as if afraid of being contaminated by poverty. After only eating half a bowl of rice, he stood up and said he was leaving. I took a lantern and gave it to him, and saw him to the door. He looked at me as if he wanted to say something but couldn't. I understood and slipped a five-yuan bill into his hand. He lowered his head, and I saw two tears slowly hanging down, hanging down. After a long time, he finally said: (Child, heaven will repay you). Then he picked up the lantern and left.

His thin shadow and that dim lantern disappeared together into the fields. (A good person!) I sighed so much.

Casual Words from Juju's Hut 212

— Zizhan

(20) Lu Xun (The Stalker of the Tang Dynasty) In Shanghai dialect, young wastrels who follow women, hooking up and teasing, are called "stalkers." Mr. Lu Xun's "Essays from the Three Idlers" has an article called "The Stalker of the Tang Dynasty," citing Zhang Bi's "Tune: Sand of the Washing Stream" tenth poem as an example, translating it into vernacular poetry. He also said that stalking may not have started in the Tang Dynasty. I think that the three poems "East Gate Pond" in the "Airs of Chen" are the oldest stalking poems. The poem says: "The pond at the east gate can soak hemp. That beautiful, virtuous woman, can I sing with her? The pond at the east gate can soak ramie. That beautiful, virtuous woman, can I talk with her? The pond at the east gate can soak rush. That beautiful, virtuous woman, can I speak with her?" If we combine the meaning of the three poems and translate them into one vernacular poem, we will get the following: "In that dirty pond at the east gate, soaking the grass for twisting ropes, soaking the hemp for spinning thread, I think both are possible. You beautiful, modern lady, can I chat with you, and sing with you: (Sister, I love you)?" I don't know what wise readers think, and what Mr. Lu Xun would think if he saw it!

Carrot Top 213

— By Jules Renard, translated by Lin Qu

Chickens

(I can bet,) Mrs. Lepic said, (Olo rine has forgotten to lock up the chickens again.) Really, we can tell from the window. Over there, at the top of that big courtyard, the little henhouse shows the black silhouette of the open door. (Felix, would you like to go lock up the chickens?) Mrs. Lepic said to the oldest of her three children. (I'm not here to take care of the chickens,) Felix said. This was a pale-faced, lazy, and cowardly child. (Then what about you, Ernestine?) (Ah! Me, Mom, I'm afraid!) Felix and Ernestine replied almost without looking up. They were lying on the table, almost forehead to forehead, looking at books with great interest. (Good heavens, how stupid I am!) Mrs. Lepic said. (I didn't think of him. Carrot Top. Go lock up the chickens!) She gave the youngest child this nickname because his hair was brownish and his face was full of freckles. Carrot Top, who was sulking under the table, stood up and murmured: (But, Mom, I'm afraid too.) (What?) Mrs. Lepic shouted, (A child this big is still afraid! That's funny. Go!) (Everyone knows; he's as brave as a he-goat,) his sister Ernestine said. (He's not afraid of anything, not afraid of anyone,) his older brother Felix said. These flattering words made Carrot Top proud, and he thought it would be shameful to fail their praise, and he secretly tried to overcome his cowardice. Seeing him hesitating, his mother said that if he didn't go, she would give him a slap. (Then at least shine a light for me,) he said. Mrs. Lepic shrugged her shoulders, and Felix smiled contemptuously. Only his sister Ernestine felt unbearable and took a candle to send him to the end of the corridor. (I'll wait for you here,) she said. But she immediately ran away in terror. Because a gust of wind shook the candlelight a few times and blew it out. At this point, Carrot Top was stunned and began to tremble in the dark. The night was so dark that he felt blind. A gust of wind blew, wrapping him like a cold blanket, as if to snatch him away. Were foxes, even jackals, not hissing between his fingers and on his cheeks? He knew that the only way at this time was to run towards the henhouse. He buried his head and darted into the darkness, groping, he touched the hook on the henhouse door. The chickens inside the house heard his footsteps and began to cluck in panic. Carrot Top shouted to them: (Don't make noise, it's me!) He closed the door and turned to run away, his legs and arms as if they had grown wings. When he ran back into the house panting and proudly, under the warmth and light, he felt as if he had taken off a heavy, muddy rag and put on a set of light, new clothes. He was smiling, elated, standing up straight, waiting for others' congratulations; and now that he was out of danger, he searched the faces of his family members for traces of the anxiety they had just shown. But his older brother Felix and sister Ernestine were nonchalantly continuing to read their books, while Mrs. Lepic said in her natural tone: (Carrot Top, from now on, you have to lock up the chickens every night!)

Commercial News

Finance Takes a Nose Dive Without Turning Back: Yesterday's Standard Gold Price Dropped Another 10 Yuan 214

Fluctuations of Fifty-Two Yuan in Half a Day

(Bank of America Fell Back, Opening Reached as High as 975 Yuan. The Rumor of Using Both Gold and Silver Arrived, and the Downturn Was Rampant Again.) The gold market, although only open for half a day yesterday, was turbulent with fluctuations of fifty-two yuan. In the early morning, foreign telegrams indicated that London's large bars, both near and far term, increased by 3.125, while the British-American exchange rate shrank by half a point, British-English fell by 3.5 points, New York silver prices dropped slightly by 1.25 points, far-term silver prices fell slightly by 2.9 li, American cotton had stabilized, and the wool market opened with a rebound and rose to 60 yuan. Bingxing attempted to limit purchases without success, Hengxing bought all goods, Run Changyu, Daxing, Yongyuan, Sheng Yong, and Yongze sold, hovering around 68-69 yuan. When Zhifeng and Yongfu Chang sold, it retreated to within 5 yuan. Afterwards, Yuanmao and Yongdai Bingxing purchased over 400 bars, Yuankangxiang also bought, reaching beyond 70 yuan. Bingxing then came to buy again, and the opening price was 973.5 yuan. Although the exchange market was tight at the start, banks were quite eager to sell, so it gradually declined from 75 yuan. The exchange market remained firm, and foreign telegrams reported that President Roosevelt, in a conversation with senators, seemed to be adding silver clauses to the inflation bill, so the downturn began. Before long, news spread in the market that 4.5 million yuan in silver was being shipped out of the city, and that a large amount was also planned for export. Several levels were broken in succession. However, because President Roosevelt said in a foreign telegram that production might be excessive after raising prices and that new methods would be sought, there was a rebound. In the end, morale was bleak, and it retreated to 23 yuan, closing at 25 yuan, with an additional 38 yuan for smelted red gold. The market situation for the half-day is recorded below.

The morning opening was 973.5 yuan, an increase of 28.5 yuan compared to the previous close. Goods opened at 74 yuan, and the opening exchange rates were all tight. The short-term British exchange rate was quoted at 1 shilling 2 pence 4375, 375 tighter than the previous close, and the American exchange rate was 22.875 yuan, 5625 tighter than the previous close. Bingxing continued to buy, raising it to 5 yuan. Yongfeng and Hengyu both sold, breaking the 70 yuan mark. This was because there were rumors from bank private telegrams that it would increase by 0.0625, and morale was unstable. Chunyuan, Yongfu Chang, Daxing Yong sold again, reaching 63.5 yuan, because in August, banks were willing to offer 24 yuan for American dollars. Continuous Rain and Unusual Cold Affect Spring Silkworms 224

Changan Changan was originally a famous silkworm area, but because silkworm farming has repeatedly failed in recent years, farmers and silkworm breeders are disheartened. This year, due to economic constraints, farmers lack the funds to purchase seeds, and the amount of feeding has sharply reduced. The silkworm seeds are mixed, with local (i.e., self-retained local seeds) and foreign (i.e., improved seeds from various seed breeding farms) each accounting for half. Since the silkworm ants were collected, there have been continuous rains for many days, and the weather has been unusually cold, resulting in unhealthy development of the silkworm ants. Although local silkworms have already gone through three sleeps, silkworm diseases are rampant. In the Yangjiadu Xuhangzhen area, most silkworm ants spit out black and yellow. In the Yuanhuazhen Jinshidun area, foreign silkworms have also developed slowly. The large groups have just completed their second sleep. Occasionally, some are stiff and cannot wake up. Silkworm breeders are generally pessimistic.

Pingyao Yuhang Pingyao and other areas used to be the most prosperous in silkworm farming. This year, due to economic stagnation, they are unable to purchase improved seeds and have risen up in opposition, resulting in riots. Therefore, those who have hatched local seeds this year (i.e., Yuhang seeds) have experienced continuous cloudy and rainy weather since the leaves opened, and the climate has been abnormal, resulting in uneven silkworm sleeps. The early groups have already gone through three sleeps, but most are stiff and cannot wake up due to the cold weather. Occasionally, some have silkworm diseases due to eating wet leaves. This disease spreads rapidly in the northwest countryside. Although the foreign silkworms in the southeast countryside are developing slowly, their shape is still good.

Page 17

Leisurely Musings

Further Discussion on the Root Cause of China's Ills (Part 2) 230

— Pu

We believe that there are two reasons for the unique maladies of China today: (1) the bankruptcy of various systems that maintain national consciousness; and (2) the gradual disappearance of the culture that sustains national independence. The institutional aspects were discussed in the previous issue, and now we will discuss the cultural aspects.

What is culture? We should first define it: The word "culture" in Western languages is CULTURE. It encompasses a nation's social customs, living habits, religious beliefs, written language, poetry, art, and so on. Not long ago, Mr. George Bernard Shaw, in a conversation with those welcoming him in Shanghai, also discussed the shortcomings of Chinese culture, even stating that China and the East have hardly any culture to speak of. He said: "Culture, according to a scientific explanation, is anything human behavior can do to increase human happiness, especially in the control of nature. In China, one can find very little culture except in the countryside. Today, China is taking from Western Europe much so-called culture that has already lost its effectiveness and harms the public." The great expression of a nation is the expression of its cultural power. For example, before the Meiji Restoration, Japan's nation also went through a period of internal and external danger, but it was able to rise up in time, with the people working together to save themselves, and Japan was able to undergo a complete restoration. Japan was restored, but its original Bushido spirit remained intact. We say that this was originally a legacy of ancient customs in China, but this kind of atmosphere representing ancient culture is gradually disappearing in China, while Japan has been able to promote this spirit into various undertakings that promote national progress. How is this possible? On the one hand, it is due to the support of the people for this custom, and on the other hand, it is due to the tireless promotion of cultural movements throughout history, directly and indirectly promoting and developing this spirit in novels, poems, and paintings.

In addition, in Soviet Russia, which practices communism, it opposes religion on the one hand, and overthrows many popular customs left over from the old system. On the other hand, it preserves all buildings of artistic value, and at the same time vigorously promotes various literary and artistic works related to civilians and workers. The government even established a special cultural committee to be responsible for research and promotion. The degree of importance attached to it is no less than that of other national defense and economic construction. We know that the organization of the Soviet Russian Communist Party is very strict, and the organization of the Red Army is also very well-trained. In terms of political power, it can be said that it is very strong, so there is no need to be afraid of anything. But why do they still pay so much attention to the promotion of art and literature? That is because all the political work of the Party can only see the superficial effects, but cannot deeply affect the hearts of the people, while literary and artistic works such as novels and poems have the function of subtle influence. A social system must have the latent power of culture to stand for a long time, otherwise it has no foundation.

The ability of a great nation with an ancient culture to continue its national life depends on whether it can maintain and develop its original cultural spirit. Now let's reflect on ourselves. What is our emerging culture? What can we be proud of, what is still bright and shining, and what represents our ancient culture of the Chinese nation today? Searching for some ancient culture from the political system, the system itself has gone bankrupt, and what political morality and integrity have long disappeared with the spirit of the system; seeking some culture from within the scope of education, the way of the gentleman left over from the autocratic system and the dignity between teachers and students have long been shattered; seeking some from the family system, the foundation of our social organization, the demise of the spirit of the family system did not begin today, and its collapse has been obvious for the past thirty years. Finally, let's try to find it in Mr. Shaw's so-called countryside and see what happens. We know that since the influx of foreign capitalism using machine production methods into China like a tide, the ancient production methods of rural culture that we have left behind for two or three thousand years have quickly disappeared and bankrupted. Especially in the past ten years, the degree of collapse has expanded day by day. In the next three to five years, it may enter the realm of complete bankruptcy, which is also unknown.

There is a relationship of mutual use and mutual transformation between systems and culture. Under a chaotic system that has lost the faith of the people, it is not easy for a new culture to be produced. At the same time, in the process of the gradual disappearance of the original culture, even if there are leaders with strong wills like Mussolini in Italy and Hitler in France, I am afraid that they cannot be sure of establishing a disciplined system. Because the establishment of a new system still needs to be based on the old system and the original culture. The bankruptcy and disappearance of the old system and culture make the production of new systems and new cultures lose their basis. As for how to save this crisis, it is not within the scope of this article to discuss, but it can be predicted that the whole country uniting and fighting to the death to seek survival is more hopeful than the current method of living in peace and waiting for death.

Skimming the Fat 231

— Qilian

They are not said to be working, but they are also selling their labor to the capitalists; if you say they are working, they are not like ordinary workers who work hard with their hands and feet. They wear uniforms provided by the company and carry white cloth bags full of copper coins on their shoulders. The weight does not seem to be heavy, but bearing it on their shoulders for eight hours without leaving their shoulders cannot be done without long-term training. This is the occupation (ticket seller) that is generally considered to be very profitable by the people of Shanghai.

Tram Ticket Sellers

In order to understand their actual living conditions, I specially went to find my friend who sells tickets one day; he told me many real situations that outsiders do not know. He said: "Looking at our industry on the surface, there is no other occupation that can compare with it; the income is high, the job does not have to be restricted by anyone, and the time is only eight hours, which is the same as working in an office. But there are unspeakable hardships in it, but no one can understand them. Passengers only know that ticket sellers make a lot of money by 'skimming the fat,' but they don't know that we are taking the price of taking a gamble with our occupation..."

"...Then why do you neglect your duties to take this undeserved profit?" I interrupted him.

"Yes! What you said is not bad, but we seem to have regarded 'skimming the fat' as a sideline. We know that doing this will break our own jobs, but we don't consider this point. What becomes a problem is whether there are passengers." He was probably excited to speak, took off his uniform and threw it aside, and continued: "Foreigners are cunning, but Chinese people are not stupid; the ticket sellers in the past were flexible in their 'skimming the fat,' and the later ones were even more inflexible."

"Then your 'sideline' can now be done more frankly? I am afraid that you can't earn more than a hundred dollars a month?" I thought I guessed correctly when I saw him looking so proud.

"Hum! More than a hundred dollars! Where did such a convenient thing come from in this world? Our wages are twenty-three dollars a month, which is just a nice cover. In fact, if you can take three or five dollars back every month, you are considered to have good skills. Unless you don't do a 'sideline,' otherwise, the fine notices posted in the office are unknown to everyone. Some new ticket sellers, of course, do not dare to do the act of 'skimming the fat' in the first few days on the bus; don't say 'skimming the fat,' they haven't even figured out the threshold of selling tickets. When they go to the company to pay the bill, either the tickets are sold wrong or the copper coins are short. But the company will never forgive these because you are a novice. Really, this kind of 'skimming the fat' sideline has now simply formed a traditional and universal idea in the company. Leisurely Coffee Corner

The Terror of Unemployment 233

— Jingxian

I went out to work in a hurry today. The food, clothing, housing, and transportation of a family of old and young are finally taken care of by the boss and have been settled. But then I think, what if I suddenly break my job tomorrow?

Eating other people's food and losing your job is as plain as a few thunderbolts in June and a snowstorm in December. It is not qualified to be compared with the news of "(one birth, three children)" and "(the dead resurrected)." Because the boss is to us clerks as we are to a cat or a dog. We have the right to stop supplying food to cats and dogs, and the boss, of course, also has the freedom to stop business with the clerks.

We clerks don't want to think about it, and that's fine. We sleep until dawn, and don't even have a nightmare. If it is unexpected and the mood strikes, we think of the terror after unemployment, and we can't even eat, and we can't even get out of bed. As soon as we put our heads on the pillow, we dream of our wives and children, crying for hunger and cold. Letters of debt collection, court summons, and rice store bills pour in like snowflakes. When we wake up in shock, the beating of the heart seems to break through the chest.

The opportunity for unemployment is lurking around us. A disagreement with customers, offending the parents of food and clothing, or bumping into Mr. A Da with a few words, I'm sorry, please pack up your luggage and find another high position. Military band, ..., ..., ..., spring big price cut, summer big bargain sale, plus ten-week anniversary, special low price, oh no, narrowing the scope, laying off staff and reducing politics, small numbers cannot accommodate large scale, so we have to find another place. Even if we rely on the spirit of Mr. Sun Yat-sen in heaven, plus the accumulation of virtue of our ancestors, our jobs are not broken in the big contraction, and we still live the life of small profits but quick turnover, 365 days a year of big price cuts. In the end, the boss has no intention of continuing to make profits. At that time, there is no way to go, and we are not afraid of not getting kicked in the ass. Sometimes, it's still fine the night before, but before dawn, "cock-a-doodle-doo," "boom," "boom," the war begins. After half a year or five months, the ceasefire agreement is signed. The boss's decades-old store, which he has worked so hard to run, has been turned into ashes. What else is there to say? Even if the world is peaceful and the market is maintained by some patriotic people, we are still unlucky. We get a cold, then a headache, then fever and chills. Zhang Long is dead, and we can't afford to hire a fashionable doctor. We lie straight on the bed and hold on. We sweat profusely every day, three bodies of small sweat. Even if we are lucky enough to get rid of the fever and chills, we have already been sick for ten and a half days. After getting out of bed, some people are as thin as firewood, and some people have no energy. At this time, the boss sends a letter saying that he will be temporarily laid off and rehired after recovery. In fact, the so-called "temporary" is just a front. To open the skylight and speak frankly, it is "(we don't want you, you sick ghost.)" But if you don't even fart, sometimes you can't even imagine losing your job. For example, the boss has just taken in a new favorite, and he will inevitably bring a group of brothers-in-law, sisters-in-law, or old friends of Mr. A Da. If they lose their jobs and have nowhere to settle down, they will all have to covet your job. These big shots (job enemies) are impossible to resist. All of these things will make you think about it and make you uneasy. As for the words "guarantee," don't even think about it, and don't dare to think about it!

crowded, the ticket is forgotten to be sold; the ticket inspector will impartially seize your evidence (?) and report to the company, and his duty for the day is considered to be completed. The company does not care about these rights and wrongs, and generally accuses you of "(skimming the fat)" and the fine is often beyond your expectations." He was no longer as proud as before; he tightened his serious face and sighed softly.

"Yes, the capital always treats employees unkindly; but if you) have never had this habit of (skimming the fat), the company will not (look for bones in an egg); even if you want to find it, I am afraid you can't find it, right?" I seemed to want to comfort him, but I couldn't help but blame him a few words.

"Wrong is wrong, but the environment forces you to do this. And there is a bad rule that encourages you to do it. The driver clearly wants money, the ticket inspector wants to eat black, the dispatcher wants regular rules, and even the people who sweep the car and pry the road have to spend money. In short, the ticket seller is the source of wealth for all kinds of employees. You have to spend money everywhere. Otherwise, you will run into walls everywhere, and everything you do will be inconvenient for you. May I ask, where can these expenses come from? Since there is no furniture to bring out of the house, what other way is there to remedy it besides (skimming the fat)?" He asked with a questioning look, tilting his head, seeming to be eager for me to give him a concrete answer.

"Um, um! But didn't you say that the ticket inspector is impartial? How can he eat black? The dispatcher doesn't need to give regular rules! Are you still afraid that he won't dispatch you to work? I don't think this is necessarily the reason for manipulating you to (skim the fat)." I still insisted on my own opinion and retorted him.

So he said: "I said that the ticket inspector is impartial, is when he checks tickets on the bus; eating black is in his house, and it has to be delivered to his house. If the dispatcher doesn't send regular rules, although he doesn't have the right not to give you a shift, if you ask for sick leave, or are late for a moment due to an accident, that is the opportunity for him to exercise the power of using public office for personal revenge; one shift is three days, not only losing wages, but also being subject to extra fines!"

Citizens' Assembly

Beware of Being Deceived 236

— Sen

At the end of the Qing Dynasty, the national situation became more and more dangerous. Internally, the corruption of politics reached its peak, and externally, the oppression of imperialism became more and more fierce. After the Sino-Japanese War, China was almost destroyed. At that time, many revolutionaries rose up to spread the revolution, wanting to overthrow the Manchu Qing rule and establish a democratic government in order to seek national liberation. The Manchu Qing government saw that this situation was unfavorable to them, so they stepped up the suppression of revolutionary forces, but they might as well make concessions to imperialism. Their slogan was: "(Rather give it to foreigners than to family slaves)." This means that they would rather lose the country than let you revolutionary people raise your heads! You see, how vicious their hearts are! At that time, there was also a group of slave running dogs who also helped the Manchu Qing government to shout: "(We cannot have a revolution, revolution is enough to destroy the country!)" However, the climax of the revolution could not be stopped after all, and the storm finally swept in. The Manchu Qing Dynasty was overthrown, and the Republic was still the Republic!

This kind of example of "(rather give it to foreigners than to family slaves)" is common in history. To give a famous example, in the Franco-Prussian War of 1870, the French army was defeated and Paris was besieged. At that time, the poorest people in Paris all rose up and joined the army, bravely resisting the enemy, but the ruling bourgeoisie and nobles saw that this vast armed force of the masses was very unfavorable to them. So they did not hesitate to cede land and pay reparations, seeking peace with Prussia, wanting to first reach a compromise with the foreign enemy and then suppress the domestic revolutionary masses. However, the masses opposed the peace, and the government did not hesitate to use violence to suppress them. Many people were massacred. After that, the government troops secretly went to the armory, planning to steal the people's weapons, but they were discovered. The revolutionary sentiment of the people became more and more aroused. The government was afraid of being surrounded by the people, so it quietly moved out of Paris and retreated to Versailles. The citizens of Paris then began to organize a new government, which was the famous Paris Commune. However, this Commune did not impose severe sanctions on the counter-revolutionary Versailles government. The counter-revolutionary government was able to calmly deploy and get the help of the enemy country to attack Paris. As a result, the Paris Commune failed, and more than 30,000 people were killed. This is a very famous event in Western history. There are many other similar cases. In general, every government, when faced with foreign aggression, may initially use the revolutionary forces of the people, but when it sees that the revolutionary forces are rising too much and are unfavorable to itself, it will turn to compromise with the enemy and do everything it can to suppress the revolutionary people in its own country. This has almost become a common practice.

After the September 18th Incident broke out, what followed the term "non-resistance doctrine" was "jointly facing the national crisis." Whether it was in the east or the west, it was "jointly facing the national crisis." From the mouths of noble people, in articles, and in all newspapers and magazines, we could almost hear and see the four words "jointly facing the national crisis" everywhere. But how to "(jointly)" face it? And who to "(jointly)" face it with? I was always a little confused. So a group of adults and gentlemen gave an explanation, saying that the (whole) people should unite, regardless of class, to "(jointly)" face the national crisis; the so-called regardless of class means that whether he is revolutionary or counter-revolutionary can be united to jointly face the national crisis; to go a step further, to face the national crisis and eliminate the counter-revolutionary elements... then it cannot be called "(jointly)". Therefore, if we want to jointly face the national crisis, we should not eliminate the counter-revolutionary elements... otherwise, our whole people cannot be (organized) and cannot jointly face the national crisis. This sounds very clever. However, can we (jointly) face the national crisis without eliminating the counter-revolutionary elements? Can the counter-revolutionary elements (jointly) face it with us? Friends! Beware of being deceived! You don't need to turn over history, just look at the facts before your eyes!

But the husband frowned and glared, he said bitterly, "(You leaked the news again! Damn thing!)"

I had difficulty defending myself and had to remain silent. "(You go back!)" the husband ordered. I had to repeat the words of the mistress teaching him to go back again. "(You don't listen to me? Can you interfere with me?)" The husband clenched his fist, and a murderous aura rushed out between his dark eyebrows. Ah! This is another terrible, furious face! I trembled and turned around, and staggered on the way back with a disappointed mood.

Ah! My frightened heart is fighting with the biting cold west wind outside! After returning to the store, the mistress did not give me dinner. She said, "(If the husband doesn't come back tonight...)" Looking at her fierce attitude, it seemed that she couldn't wait to bite off a piece of my flesh! It was late at night, and the clock on the wall was already twelve twenty! My master came back, so my dinner problem was finally solved.

Hero's Daily Life Notes

Four Faces 237

— Ge Lang

(That Foreman) (Little Tu’s wife, after arriving in Shanghai, heard that she had not even worked for two years at the yarn factory before being promoted to (That Foreman). Her current wage is more than thirty yuan a month. Little Tu is truly blessed; now he can rely on his wife for food. He also ran to Shanghai the day before yesterday.) The neighbor, Old Wang, smacked his lips in envy to his wife. (Shanghai is indeed different from the countryside; it's easier to earn money. Just think: thirty-odd yuan; a woman working as a maid in the countryside would have to work for a year to earn that!) Aunt Wang, sewing the shoe upper in her hands, nodded in agreement, also expressing her envy!

However, I can swear that Little Tu’s arrival in Shanghai this time definitely did not have the thought of relying on his wife for food, but only wanted to find a better job. Little Tu circled Shanghai for a full two months, but still couldn’t find a job. The twenty-five yuan from selling five stones of grain was used up! Unable to go home, he had no choice but to live under his wife’s eaves, helping with cooking, washing dishes, fetching water... After five o'clock, the sky was still not bright. Little Tu got up, fanned the charcoal stove red, cooked the rice, fetched the water, and then lay beside the pillow, gently waking his wife.

As soon as she got up, she polished her high-heeled leather shoes for five minutes, then washed her face, applied snow cream, looked at herself in the mirror a few times, took a bowl and sipped a few mouthfuls, put on her coat and prepared to go to the factory. (The weather outside is bad; do you need to take an umbrella?) Little Tu said quietly while wiping the table. (Is the person not dead yet? Can’t I bring it to the factory myself?) she said, slammed the door shut with a (bang), and walked away by herself.

Highway Robber 238

— Ms. Meng Hua

Foreman

This day was the end of the month, and our factory was paying wages. I followed my fellow workers to the accounting office to collect my wages and walked out the door, where I ran into that foreman. He blocked me like a highway robber and asked: (How much wage did you collect today?) Suddenly, I was so frightened by his question that I stared blankly, not daring to answer. Seeing that I didn’t respond, he thought I was doing it on purpose and said even more fiercely: (You won’t tell me, huh!) Seeing his fierce eyes, I was really scared out of my wits! Later, I finally stuttered, (Sir…I…I only collected five yuan.) (Do you understand?) He stared at me intently.)

So I had no choice but to untie my handkerchief and hand him two yuan. (I don’t want it! I’ll give you a hard time tomorrow!) He threw the money on the ground, seeming to think it was still too little. (Sir, this is just for you to buy some cigarettes to smoke; it doesn't count as respect.) (Who wants your cigarettes!) Then, Sir…I) I endured the pain and took out another yuan to give him. He finally accepted it. (Alas! More than half a month's worth of blood and sweat, and the price I got for it was actually so cruel, so meager!) On the way home, I kept thinking about this.

Truly! Little Tu's wife's face, from entering the world until now, has indeed had four different appearances in total. The first one everyone hasn't seen, because she hasn't come to Shanghai yet; the second one is what she just showed Little Tu personally; as for the third and fourth, of course the yarn factory must be her background.

Amateur Sports

Fitness Bow 240

— Cheng Xiyuan

Neither being too thin nor too fat is a healthy phenomenon, and exercise really has the effect of improving unevenness in body fat. Because body movement is performed by the action of muscles, the more the muscles are used, the stronger and denser their texture becomes, the elasticity increases, and the fibers gradually proliferate. At the same time, it can make fat disappear, so the muscles of people who do not exercise are soft and weak, thus reducing their ability to work, which is also closely related to life.

As for the method of developing muscles, it is best to do strenuous exercise, such as wrestling, jujutsu, and lifting heavy objects. However, wrestling requires considerable comrades; jujutsu requires someone to guide you: iron dumbbells, stone weights, fitness chains, etc. can of course solve everything for those whose finances are not a problem; but for people with limited income and not very generous finances, it is difficult. Therefore, we have to think of a reformed and economical exercise equipment to remedy this regret. I remember that the previous issues of this journal once published an article by Mr. Hui Zun called (Poor Man's Equipment). Although this method is still usable, it costs more than one yuan, which is still a bit uneconomical, and the procedures are troublesome, the method of use is not varied, and installing it on the ceiling is not only unsightly, but also too rigid, so I think it is not a very good method. Now I have made something that can be used as a fitness chain. The method of making it is as follows:

(Materials) Two five-foot-long large bamboo boards (choose those that are elastic and have no cracks), two one-foot-long and two-inch-wide bamboo boards, four screw rings, one foot of thick lead wire, and several feet of rattan bark (hemp rope is also good).

(Manufacturing method) First, smooth the arc of the two five-foot-long bamboo boards on the bamboo white side (the opposite side of the bamboo green) (otherwise they will definitely break), making two bamboo boards that are two inches wide and half an inch thick. Then tie each of the two one-foot-long bamboo boards tightly to the center section of the five-foot-long bamboo board with rattan bark on the bamboo white side. As shown in Figure 1: Then, screw one of the four screw rings firmly at each end of each bamboo board, as shown in Figure 2: Then, use thick lead wire to connect each screw ring to each other, as shown in Figure 3. In this way, it is successful. (Usage) It is similar to a fitness chain and can form various postures, stretching the muscles. Hold the two hand grips (see Figure 3) with both hands and force them apart to both sides. Such as left and right bow stance (see Figure 4), backhand pull, level split, split upwards, lift from bottom to top, pull down from top to bottom, and other various postures. In short, you have to change it according to your own ideas; there is no fixed rule; but the point to note is that you must not specialize in one-sided exercises, which will hinder balanced development.

Our company now needs a student interested in the new drug industry, qualified with a high school degree and able to endure hardship. Contact Bailing Drug Store at the corner of Sixth Road and Yunnan Road.

According to the above method, the cost is only about half a yuan, which is naturally more economical compared to (Poor Man's Equipment). If you can spend a little more effort to make it more sophisticated, it will be very beautiful. It is also easy to use and does not have to be limited to a fixed place. You can practice indoors or outdoors. Although it cannot increase the weight, it can increase the number of times, which is still the same in comparison. It seems that this thing has not been seen outside, because its function is similar to that of a fitness chain, so it is called (Fitness Bow).

Monograph

A Class of European and American Unemployment Relief Policies 243

— Jing

Unemployment is the inevitable result of capitalism. In capitalist society, its economic organization is built on the interests of capitalists. Therefore, all hired laborers can only sell their labor power on the condition that it is beneficial to their employer capitalists; otherwise, they must often depend on the convenience of the employer, who can dismiss them at any time, and become unemployed. Because from the employer's point of view, this is necessary to maintain the interests of their industry, so the unemployed can only live their miserable lives. At this time, the state does not guarantee the financial resources for the lives of the unemployed, society has no obligation to support them, and trade unions have no long-term financial resources to support them. It can be said that they have neither a self-defense strategy nor the right to force others to come to their aid, but only to find their own way out.

From this point of view, the phenomenon of unemployment is of course absolutely unfavorable to laborers, but the continuous increase in the number of unemployed is also enough to make society uneasy, disrupt social order, and affect the capitalists' industries, causing them to suffer disadvantages. Therefore, capitalists have to think of various methods to seek remedies in order to avoid this unfavorable phenomenon. But can this kind of remedy be effective? We only need to take a look at their so-called relief policies. Let's take the advanced capitalist countries of Europe and America as examples. In European and American countries, there are different unemployment relief strategies, but they can generally be divided into the following three types: (1) Employment agencies. The operators of employment agencies, in addition to individual for-profit businesses, also include (1) employer groups; (2) labor unions; (3) charitable or public groups; (4) municipal or national agencies. Because the expansion of unemployment is often general, it is not easy to achieve relief unless employment agencies are widely established in various places and a unified agency is established at the same time to connect and manage them. Currently, only the United Kingdom and Germany have this unified system. In France, although there is such a provision in the law, it has not yet been implemented.

(2) Unemployment insurance. This system was first created in Ghent, Belgium in 1901, and later spread to France, Germany, the Netherlands, and Denmark. Now, the implementation of Ghent in 1921, the originator, is listed as follows: (1) Municipal unemployment fund, which is for registered trade unions, based on the amount of unemployment benefits paid to their members as a standard, and give a certain subsidy; (2) The amount of the subsidy is limited to two francs per person per day, and must not exceed ten days for the same person; (3) A certificate is submitted by its former employer and employment agency to prove that the unemployment was not due to one's own intention as a condition for granting the subsidy; (4) The trade union first pays the unemployment benefits and subsidies to the unemployed, and then settles once a month and requests the subsidy from the city; (5) Regarding the economics of unemployment insurance, the trade union clarifies this and keeps a special account book to be inspected by the city. In addition, there is also national mandatory unemployment insurance, which is currently only implemented in the United Kingdom, Italy, and Austria.

(3) Restrictions on dismissal. This system began after the war. Its intention is to restrain the crowding out of the unemployed and make it easier for the unemployed to find jobs. For example: (1) Application for dismissal. When the employer intends to dismiss employees due to business closure or reduction, they must first apply to the government; (2) Notice of dismissal, which obliges the employer to give notice in advance for a certain period of time when dismissing an employee, depending on the length of service of the employee; (3) Payment of dismissal allowance, which obliges the employer to pay a certain allowance when dismissing an employee, the amount of which is based on the length of service.

The above is considered the only relief policy in Europe and America. We only need to look at recent years, especially in the current third stage of capitalism, the sharp increase in unemployment in various countries has reached an acute level, and we can know that this relief policy is ineffective. At best, it is a palliative method that can only relieve a certain part of the unemployed temporarily, but cannot fundamentally solve the unemployment problem. Our country of course need not be mentioned; we do not even have this palliative relief policy, but hasn't unemployment become a terrible phenomenon? But is there really no way to save unemployment? Is unemployment destined for laborers? No, definitely not. There is a way to save it, but it is not the kind of relief policy in Europe and America mentioned above, which only relieves it on the surface, but to think about it from the root, that is, to destroy the capitalist economic organization that produces this unemployment, and replace it with an economic organization that is opposite to it. Laborers can only be free from the danger of unemployment in this economic organization, and the unemployment problem can be fundamentally solved from then on.

Movie Special

Greta Garbo Will Not Return to Hollywood 244

— Zhu Xian

(Has a Strong Desire to Dedicate Herself to the Stage)

The Swedish strange star Greta Garbo now has two paths to take: one is to continue to engage in the film industry, which means she must return to Hollywood, because only Hollywood can afford the heavy salary, and only Hollywood is willing to pay such high wages. The other path is to give up the life of the screen and engage in stage plays. These two paths cannot be close to each other, so Garbo has already spent a lot of effort in choosing. It is said that she has recently decided to appear on stage. Of course, her choice was not obtained by drawing lots at the City God Temple; she must have her reasons. Let's discuss it briefly now: Greta Garbo has a great ambition. She believes that the world on the screen has been conquered by her. The second world she wants to conquer is the stage. With this ambition, she would rather sacrifice everything. The first is in terms of income. The stage cannot give her even one-tenth of the salary she can get on the screen. But the stage also has other rewards that the screen cannot give.

In movies, the relationship between actors and the audience is indirect. Although Garbo has already gained fame on the screen, she always feels that she has not seen or heard the direct reaction of the audience. So if she can personally step onto the stage, she can see the expressions of joy, anger, sorrow, and happiness of thousands of people responding to the stage under the footlights. She can also hear the sounds of their praise and applause. Although she used to try her best to avoid the entanglement of the crowd, now that she has this ambition, she feels that avoiding the crowd is meaningless and cowardly. Therefore, she often goes out and walks around in the capital of Sweden to get used to it. It is said that she is no longer afraid of the crowd.

In addition, there is a very big reason, which is the three words (not convinced). This is a long story. It was probably around 1920 that she graduated from the Royal Academy of Dramatic Art in the capital of Sweden. At that time, general drama playwrights did not pay attention to her dramatic talent. So a group of classmates were hired by various companies after graduation. Only this Garbo was not asked about. This is a matter that she has been ashamed of in her life. Therefore, she now wants to perform on stage to prove the mistake of those drama producers at that time. To put it in Shanghai dialect, she wants to show them some color.

When Garbo had not yet achieved her ambition, there was only one person who looked up to her and knew her talent and her possibilities. They went from being casual acquaintances to becoming very close friends. He changed her name. She used to be called Greta Gustafsson, which was too cumbersome and unpleasant to hear. He named her Greta Garbo. (Garbo) is a kind of candy in Sweden that children like to eat very much. He gave her this name in order to make it easy to remember and sound good. Later, Mr. Stiller's reputation was known to Hollywood, so they sent someone to hire him. But he strangely put forward a condition that if he was to be hired, he must also hire this unknown Ms. Garbo. Hollywood had no choice but to agree to the request. But her salary when she first arrived in Hollywood was only one or two hundred dollars a week, which seemed not worth it. Before this, Garbo had also performed in German film companies, but the cameramen always said that it was difficult to shoot her scenes, because she looked too ugly on camera. When she arrived in Hollywood, the cameraman at first had no way to put this Garbo, who was full of freckles and had a heavy body, on camera. Later, thanks to the hairdressers, tailors, beauticians, makeup artists, and photographers who joined forces to completely transform her before she could be put on camera. When the first film was completed, she had smooth sailing and became a top star in Hollywood.

Movie Review

Review of (The King of the Jungle) THE KING OF JUNGLE 245

— Ling He

The products under the capitalist system are always indispensable for a form of competition with each other. Although it is not necessarily based on the principle of (comparing goods with goods), once there is a certain product that can make money, then you must come up with something similar. This means that at least you can compete with it. This is completely opposite to the socialist system with controlled production.

In terms of film production, this phenomenon is also very clear, especially in American films. If someone makes a film with horse racing as the subject matter, everyone will imitate it, so (horse racing) fills the film market. Similarly, not long ago there was (Tarzan the Ape Man), so now there is also (The King of the Jungle). Of course, the content of these two films is bound to be largely the same.

The above may be what should be pointed out before the article. Now let's turn to the main text.

If we have to make a more strict critique of this film, then the first thing to point out is the distortion of consciousness. We see that the so-called (LION MAN) protagonist KASPA is conquered by both white people and lions, and is played with by civilized people in civilized cities. Later, he finally envies the uncivilized mountains and forests of Africa, cannot leave his wild animal companions, resolutely takes his lover back to the mountains and forests, and resumes that barbaric life. Regarding this point, it is obvious that it wants to restore human beings to the primitive era, at least sympathizing with (humans and lions being together), becoming a kind of regressive and reactionary thing. Moreover, the story itself is also very fantastic. No one can believe that a two- or three-year-old child can actually survive alone from a pile of bones without being harmed by a group of lions, even though he can be friendly with lions when he grows up. As for sympathizing with lions and hating humans, this kind of cynical fantasy can actually occur in the West where material civilization has reached its extreme, which is really astonishing.

It is very clear here that the producers of this film have completely failed to recognize that films should have their educational significance. On the contrary, if they could introduce the primitive life of Africa faithfully and add correct explanations, as well as introduce rare zoological knowledge to the general audience on the screen in a learning and educational way, then this kind of film would have its value.

As mentioned above, this film is an anti-scientific work, undoubtedly a myth-like thing. In the United States, which prides itself on scientific civilization, there is actually this phenomenon, although it is relatively small, but we admit that it is a disgrace to mankind. As for the brutal behavior of white people oppressing natives on the screen, it is an exposure of themselves.

But in terms of technique, American film producers often succeed by relying on large capital. For example, the director can use fire and the riot or fighting of wild beasts to make this film a good harvest; but it seems that I don't need to explain it. Also, a swimmer inevitably becoming a tool of capitalist production is also worth our attention.

Review Two 246

— Yan Nan

Yesterday, the simultaneous release of (King of the Jungle) at both the Grand Theater and the Lyceum Theater caused quite a stir. This shows that people's special interest in this kind of hunting film has not diminished in the slightest. In terms of the story, it is quite similar to (Tarzan the Ape Man). It tells the story of a child who went to Africa with a hunting team a long time ago. Later, the entire team was wiped out, and only the child survived. He grew up among lions and was called "Lion" by the natives. Once, a white hunting team set a trap, and (Lion Man) and several lions were all captured. He was sold to an American circus. The Lion Man escaped once and met a young woman. Although they could not communicate verbally, they were in love with each other. The circus owner used the female lead, one scene from the famous European film (Good Earth), a joint production of German and English film companies. It is a grand opera with a wealth of beauty and power. The male lead, Jack Puella, is a rising star in Europe. The film was well received when it premiered in Europe and America. It is said that the film has been shipped to Shanghai and will soon be released in Shanghai. The woman used culture to enlighten the Lion Man, teaching him language and etiquette. Eventually, the woman and the Lion Man got married. Although the Lion Man had been influenced by culture, he longed to return to Africa to live an uncivilized life. So, the couple bought back some of the most docile lions from the circus and went to the lions' den in Africa together.

In terms of the plot, it seems too far-fetched. And the ideological contradictions have been exposed without reservation. According to the story, we humans should not have culture, and civilized life is not as simple and free as the lives of beasts. Then what reason do we have to demand culture? Why oppose the barbaric life of ancient times? And why have a film industry born out of culture?

The loopholes in the performance are more numerous than in (Tarzan the Ape Man) or (Freaks). In terms of directing skills, although he has tried his best to be flexible, his negligence is also undeniable. For example, within a few days, the Lion Man was able to speak fluent English, which is not reasonable. The Lion Man's escape from the circus and the buying back of the lions are completely done in the dark, which is also very vague. Also, the circus fire did not spread slowly; it was as if people were setting fires on all sides. The style is still novel, continuously describing the African lions and tigers and the circus, which is very natural and unprecedented in previous animal films. However, from beginning to end, there are only large groups of lions and a lack of other wild animals. There are also very few circus performances, which ultimately feels like a flaw.

The most important thing about this type of film is the location shooting. Its grandeur of location shooting is unmatched by other films. The photography is also good, and the clever angles of the camera make the sunlight beautiful. The editing is also seamless, constantly making people feel nervous. The beginning depicts the child's survival, and then the Lion Man, unlike the sudden appearance of the ape-man in (Tarzan the Ape Man). The first few scenes and the fire scene are the highlights of this film. Apart from the lack of awareness, the overall structure is not very far-fetched.

The protagonist, the Lion Man, is swimmer Buster Crabbe's debut on the screen, and the performance is good. The first half is excellent, but the second half is too gentle, which is not very consistent with the wildness that has not been eliminated in the play. This should be blamed on the director. The female lead, Frances Dee, has the best expressions in the whole play, and the kind of lingering affection is really something that only an experienced performer can do. The rest, only Robert Barrron, Nie Xosby, and Patricia Farley have brief but good performances. This film is very suitable for those who (watch movies for the sake of watching movies). It has good art to appreciate, and it has a pleasant performance story that makes people happy... If you are satisfied with (Tarzan the Ape Man), then I dare to recommend you to go.

Paramount has succeeded, but I think this film will disappoint some people who have too high expectations.

### The Competition of Hollywood Clothes 247

— Shi Chun

In this bustling area of Hollywood, divorce and marriage are a big fuss. Therefore, the three necessities of life, clothing, food, and shelter, have also become various patterns, providing good materials for newspaper reporters in magazines and newspapers. Recently, there has been another clothing competition in Hollywood, which is even more sensational.

The leaders of the clothing competition are all wealthy stars in Hollywood. The first is Constance Bennett. The second is Katharine Hepburn. The third is Lee Sidah Heemen.

The method of competition is to wear clothes that are as fashionable as possible. The fashionable styles take the Paris market as the standard. The faster the news, the more fashionable the clothes worn. Often, the styles change after one or two hours. So those who get the news slowly fall behind. All three of them have special contracts with radio stations in Paris to provide them with the fastest news.

Each of them tried their best to influence the news media to publish more of their criticisms. But there is no definitive answer as to who is the best.

### Film Novel Cavalcade (5) 248

— Ne

The audience in the theater was overjoyed to hear this news. The women were overly happy, not knowing whether to cry or laugh, but they were moved in their hearts, and tears welled up in their eyes as they walked out of the theater. Keane and Margaret were also among the crowd, walking and singing on the road like a tide. Margaret danced a waltz on the road. But there was also a terrible thing, which was the list of soldiers' casualties published in the newspapers every day. The first time, they quickly looked through it, and the second time, they carefully and fearfully checked it again, fearing that they had missed an important name in the first moment of negligence. Keane looked through it line by line, and when she saw that there was no Robert Mayo's name in a line, her heart felt like a big stone falling to the ground. Soon Robert returned in triumph.

Although Robert survived, the affairs of the world after that were like a revolving lantern, changing endlessly one after another. The first and most memorable thing was the death of Queen Victoria. Keane still remembered the people standing quietly outside Buckingham Palace late at night, waiting for the announcement of the Queen's condition. Every day, she read the news in the newspaper that the Queen was about to die, and felt something stuck in her throat, but Bridges stood respectfully beside her and said: "Even without the Queen, Britain will still be fine." Later, the Queen died, and Keane and her children watched the funeral procession passing through the street from the balcony. Joey suddenly asked his mother: "Why did Queen Victoria have to die?" Keane looked at her little son with tears in her eyes and said: "Because she is very, very old and too tired." The soldiers slowly passed by, and the two children saw their father leading the way and whispering to each other. Victoria's coffin was displayed on a gun carriage, so small that it looked like a child's coffin. Joey said to his mother again: "She must have been very small when she was alive." Keane quickly said: "She is very great. Don't you see five kings behind her, riding horses behind her?"

The Victorian era has come to an end, and Edward has ascended the throne. The current Britain is a completely different world. Robert has been knighted. The two children have grown up. Bridges and Ellen have left their employers to open a hotel. In the beginning, Keane often took the children to see them. Fanny's small figure was as beautiful as a flower. But Bridges was addicted to alcohol, and Ellen tried her best to hide it. They opened their own shop and had broken away from the servant class, so they were even more arrogant than ordinary people. Keane gradually dared not go again. After a while, Keane no longer asked about this pair of old and trusted servants. So she did not know that Fanny was gradually attracted to many playboys, and she also heard nothing about Bridges being killed. (To be continued)
